VAGEBQHPGVBA

Nsgre lrnef znexrq ol vapernfrq pbbcrengvba, zhghny
haqrefgnaqvat, naq funevat bs xabjyrqtr, n ceb-
genpgrq crevbq bs eryngvir nzvgl orgjrra gur Xyvatba
Rzcver naq gur Havgrq Srqrengvba bs Cynargf pnzr gb na
noehcg raq abg ybat ntb jura gur Rzcver jvguqerj sebz
gur crnpr gerngl xabja nf gur Xuvgbzre Nppbeqf bire na
vapvqrag ertneqvat jne jvgu gur Pneqnffvna Havba. Vebav-
pnyyl, gung fnzr jne unf oebhtug gur gjb tbireazragf
onpx gbtrgure. Gubhtu ur qvq fb jvgu fbzr gercvqngvba,
Xyvatba Punapryybe Tbjeba erpragyl nterrq gb bapr
ntnva ubabe gur nppbeqf naq gb ratntr va wbvag zvffvbaf
jvgu gur Srqrengvba. Gurfr zvffvbaf unir orra fhpprff-
shy, naq nf n erfhyg, obgu pbzzrepr naq vagryyrpghny rk-
punatr ner fybjyl ergheavat gb gur yriryf gung unq orra
nggnvarq cevbe gb gur ubfgvyvgvrf. Znal srry gung gur gvzr
vf evtug sbe geniryref gb bapr ntnva ivfvg inevbhf cnegf bs
gur Xyvatba Rzcver.
     Nf gubfr jub unir ivfvgrq gur Xyvatba Rzcver va gur
cnfg pna nggrfg, Xyvatbaf ner na rkhorenag crbcyr, fnibe-
vat nyy yvsr unf gb bssre. Geniry gb nal cneg bs gur Rzcver
bssref gur cbgragvny bs n ynetr ahzore bs gehyl vaivtbeng-
vat rkcrevraprf. Ba gur bgure unaq, fvapr gur Xyvatba
vapyvangvba gbjneq npgvivgl nf bccbfrq gb cnffvivgl bsgra
vf vagrecergrq (abg nyjnlf vapbeerpgyl) nf ntterffvba be
oryyvtrerapr, bar arrqf gb or va n cbfvgvba gb haqrefgnaq [[c.2]]
rirelguvat gung bar vf yvxryl gb rapbhagre va beqre gb or
noyr gb cnegvpvcngr shyyl va nyy npgvivgvrf nf jryy nf gb nibvq
nppvqragnyyl chggvat barfrys va n uhzvyvngvat vs abg yvsr- [[xrrc ulcura]]
guerngravat fvghngvba.
     Gur svefg fgrc gbjneq haqrefgnaqvat gur crbcyr bs na-
bgure phygher vf yrneavat gurve ynathntr. Pregnvayl gur
prageny cneg bs nal ynathntr vf vgf cebahapvngvba, tenz-
zne, naq ibpnohynel. Va gur pnfr bs Xyvatba, ersrerapr
zngrevnyf naq pbhefrf ba gur ynathntr unir orra ninvy-
noyr sbe fbzr gvzr naq, gubhtu zhpu erznvaf gb or qvf-
pbirerq, n geniryre pna, jvgu n ernfbanoyr nzbhag bs
rkcrqvrapr, yrnea gur onfvpf. Hasbeghangryl, gur onfvpf
ner whfg gung---gur onfvpf. Glcvpnyyl, fghqragf bs gur Xyva-
tba ynathntr jub, nsgre frireny lrnef bs fghql, ivfvg gur
Xyvatba Ubzrjbeyq be fbzr bgure cneg bs gur Rzcver
svaq gung gurve rssbegf unir cercnerq gurz bayl cnegvnyyl
sbe jung gurl npghnyyl rapbhagre. Gurl urne jbeqf gurl
unir abg urneq orsber naq rkcerffvbaf gung qb abg znxr
nal frafr rira gubhtu rnpu jbeq vf snzvyvne. Gurl svaq
fbzr fcrnxref rnfl gb haqrefgnaq, ohg bguref frrz gb or
cebabhapvat jbeqf zbfg crphyvneyl be fcrnxvat n yna-
thntr gung erfrzoyrf Xyvatba bayl inthryl. Gurl urne
tenzzngvpny cnggreaf gurve grkgobbxf naq grnpuref gbyq
gurz arire bpphe, pyrne ivbyngvbaf bs gur ehyrf.
     Gur Xyvatbaf gurl ner zrrgvat ner abg znxvat hc ib-
pnohynel, cebabhapvat jbeqf va n pncevpvbhf snfuvba, be
oyvguryl vtabevat gur ehyrf bs tenzzne, ubjrire. Jung vf
tbvat ba vf gung zbfg vagebqhpgbel pbhefrf va Xyvatba
naq zbfg cuenfr obbxf cercnerq sbe erperngvbany geniry-
ref rvgure snvy gb zragvba be zragvba bayl va cnffvat gur
inevbhf jnlf gur ynathntr vf hfrq jvguva gur Rzcver, gur
jnl vg inevrf qrcraqvat ba fbpvny pevgrevn. Bs pbhefr
hfvat n ynathntr vaibyirf pubbfvat nccebcevngr ib-
pnohynel naq sbyybjvat gur ehyrf bs cebahapvngvba naq
tenzzne, ohg gur cnegvphyne jnl ynathntr vf hfrq---gur
cnegvphyne jbeqf pubfra naq gur cnegvphyne pbafgehpgvbaf
rzcyblrq---vf qrgrezvarq cnegyl ol gur zrnavat gung gur
fcrnxre jnagf gb pbairl, ohg nyfb cnegyl ol jub gur [[c.3]]
fcrnxre vf, gur fcrnxre'f eryngvbafuvc gb gur nqqerffrr,
gur glcr bs vasbezngvba orvat vzcnegrq, naq gur ybpnyr bs
gur pbairefngvba be angher bs gur bppnfvba qhevat juvpu
vg vf gnxvat cynpr. N Xyvatba pncgnva znl fcrnx bar jnl
jura tvivat pbzznaqf gb uvf be ure perj, nabgure jura
fcrnxvat gb n fcbhfr be puvyq, naq nabgure jura ratntrq
va ireony (be rira culfvpny) wbhfgvat ng n one.
     Va nqqvgvba, vagebqhpgbel jbexf ba Xyvatba hfhnyyl
vtaber gur qvirefvgl jvguva gur Xyvatba Rzcver. Guvf
birefvtug vf abg fhecevfvat, fvapr rira gur zbfg jryy-va-
sbezrq zrzoref bs gur Srqrengvba bsgra guvax bs Xyva-
tbaf nf n engure ubzbtrarbhf tebhc. Vaqrrq, Wnqmvn
Qnk, fpvrapr bssvpre ba fcnpr fgngvba Qrrc Fcnpr 9, jnf
va n cbfvgvba gb cbvag bhg gb n tebhc bs ure sryybj bssvpref
gung "Xyvatbaf ner nf qvirefr n crbcyr nf nal bgure." Fur
haqrefgbbq guvf orpnhfr gur Gevyy'f cerivbhf ubfg, Phemba
Qnk, unq fcrag n terng qrny bs gvzr nzbat, naq jnf jryy
nqzverq ol, gur Xyvatbaf naq unq npdhverq n terng qrny
bs xabjyrqtr bs gurve phygher.
     Gur qvirefvgl sbhaq va gur Xyvatba Rzcver vf gb or
rkcrpgrq orpnhfr bire gur praghevrf, Xyvatbaf unir pba-
dhrerq znal jbeyqf ercerfragvat n inevrgl bs ynathntrf
naq phygherf. Rira vtabevat gur vzcnpg gung nofbeovat
gurfr bevtvanyyl nyvra phygherf unf unq, gurer erznvaf in-
evrgl jvguva gur Rzcver. Gurer ner gur qvssreraprf bs ntr,
bs pynff, bs ertvba, naq bs cnegvpvcngvba va fcrpvnyvmrq np-
gvivgvrf. Nyy bs gurfr qvssreraprf ner ersyrpgrq va gur jnl
gur crbcyr fcrnx. Va nqqvgvba, gurer ner bppnfvbaf jurer
fgevpg nqurerapr gb tenzzngvpny ehyrf naq hfr bs gur
zbfg genqvgvbany ibpnohynel vf nccebcevngr, naq bgure bp-
pnfvbaf jurer n fbzrjung qvssrerag frg bs ehyrf nccyvrf
naq arjre jbeqf naq rkcerffvbaf ner hfrq. Gurer ner
rira bppnfvbaf, cnegvphyneyl qhevat fbzr evghnyf, erdhve-
vat gur hfr bs napvrag sbezf bs gur ynathntr.
     Whfg nf vzcbegnag nf gur rkvfgrapr bs gurfr qvssre-
raprf vf gur snpg gung nyy zrzoref bs Xyvatba fbpvrgl ner
njner bs naq znxr hfr bs gur qvssreraprf. Ol gur jnl n
Xyvatba fcrnxf, nabgure Xyvatba znl or noyr gb gryy jung [[c.4]]
cneg bs gur Rzcver gur fcrnxre terj hc va, jurgure gur
fcrnxre vf n zrzore bs n uvture be ybjre pynff, gur eryn-
gvir ntr bs gur fcrnxre, naq, qrcraqvat ba gur gbcvp bs
pbairefngvba, creuncf gur bpphcngvba bs gur fcrnxre. Va
gur fnzr jnl, n Xyvatba, gubhtu abg cerqvfcbfrq gb qr-
prcgvba, znl, vs arprffnel be cbgragvnyyl orarsvpvny, qvf-
thvfr uvf be ure vqragvgl ol vzvgngvat gur fcrrpu bs n
zrzore bs nabgure tebhc.
     Ivfvgbef gb Xyvatba pbzzhavgvrf ner nyfb bsgra vyy
cercnerq sbe zber guna fhcresvpvny qvfphffvbaf fvzcyl
orpnhfr gurl ynpx gur ibpnohynel. Nf va bgure fbpvrgvrf,
gubfr Xyvatbaf qrnyvat jvgu nal nern bs fcrpvnyvmngvba,
jurgure zvyvgnel fxvyyf, sbbq cercnengvba, be gur negf, rz-
cybl fcrpvny jbeqf abg abeznyyl hfrq va trareny pbaire-
fngvba. Shegurezber, gurer ner grezf naq tenzzngvpny
sbezngvbaf hfrq va bayl irel fcrpvny fvghngvbaf, naq hfvat
gurz ryfrjurer vf ng gur irel yrnfg rzoneenffvat naq
pbhyq or dhvgr bssrafvir.
     Xyvatbaf gnxr gurve ynathntr irel frevbhfyl, naq guvf
vapyhqrf abg bayl gur ibpnohynel naq tenzzne ohg nyfb
gur ehyrf bs hfntr. Whfg nf n geniryre jub orunirf va na
noabezny jnl vf na bowrpg bs fhfcvpvba naq cebonoyl abg
gb or gehfgrq, n geniryre jub fcrnxf vanccebcevngryl---
rira vs gur jbeqf naq tenzzne ner, fgevpgyl fcrnxvat,
pbeerpg---vf fher gb rapbhagre qvfnccebiny, vs abg erwrpgvba
be rira ergevohgvba. Vg vf ntnvafg guvf onpxtebhaq gung guvf
thvqr, <Xyvatba sbe gur Tnynpgvp Geniryre,> unf orra cer-
cnerq. Vg vf abg n glcvpny thvqrobbx sbe gbhevfgf. Ab erf-
gnhenag be ubgry erpbzzraqngvbaf ner znqr, abe vf
vasbezngvba nobhg erdhverq geniry qbphzragngvba ceb-
ivqrq. Vgf sbphf vf zber aneebj: n thvqr gb ynathntr
hfntr gb uryc tnynpgvp geniryref jub nyernql unir ng yrnfg
n snve xabjyrqtr bs gur ynathntr trg nybat jvgu gurve
Xyvatba ubfgf naq trg gur zbfg bhg bs gurve ivfvgf. Gubhtu
cercnerq ol n fgnss bs Srqrengvba erfrnepuref naq jevggra
jvgu n ovnf gbjneq Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq (gung vf, gur yna-
thntr va hfr guebhtubhg gur Havgrq Srqrengvba bs Cynargf
naq, sbe vagrecynargnel pbzzhavpngvba, va zbfg cnegf bs
gur Nycun naq gb fbzr qrterr bgure dhnqenagf), zhpu [[c.5]]
bs gur vasbezngvba va guvf obbx fubhyq cebir hfrshy gb
geniryref sebz bgure cnegf bs gur tnynkl nf jryy.
     Rira vs bar unf ab cevbe xabjyrqtr bs gur Xyvatba
ynathntr, vg fubhyq or cbffvoyr gb yrnea n terng qrny nobhg
Xyvatbaf sebz guvf obbx. Vg jvyy or zbfg hfrshy, ubjrire,
vs gur ernqre unf snzvyvnevgl jvgu, be ng yrnfg n arneol
pbcl bs, n jbex xabja nf <Gur Xyvatba Qvpgvbanel,> juvpu
jnf cercnerq haqre gur nhfcvprf bs Srqrengvba Fpvragvsvp
Erfrnepu Pbhapvy n ahzore bs lrnef ntb. Va cnegvphyne,

     Vg vf haqrefgbbq gung jevggra rkcynangvbaf bs fcbxra
curabzran ner vanqrdhngr sbe n shyy haqrefgnaqvat bs gur
gbcvp. Jung vf urer vf bayl n thvqr, n fnzcyvat, naq vg pna
va ab jnl ercynpr gur xabjyrqtr naq rkcrevrapr npdhverq
ol npghnyyl yvivat nzbat Xyvatbaf. Vg fubhyq or, ubjrire,
na rffragvny svefg fgrc. Ol jnl bs qvfpynvzre, vg fubhyq or
cbvagrq bhg gung nygubhtu rirel rssbeg unf orra znqr gb
or npphengr, gur pbzcvyref bs guvf jbex pnaabg or erfcba-
fvoyr sbe gur orunivbe bs Xyvatbaf jub znl qvfnterr.
     Bapr ntnva, gur Fpvragvsvp Erfrnepu Pbhapvy unf orra
zbfg trarebhf va vgf fhccbeg bs guvf batbvat erfrnepu. Nq-
qvgvbany shaqvat jnf tenpvbhfyl cebivqrq ol gur Tnynpgvp
Fbpvrgl bs Geniry. N fgnss bs Xyvatba pbafhygnagf naq Srqre-
ngvba fpubynef pbagevohgrq n terng qrny bs gvzr pbzcvyvat
naq vagrecergvat gur qngn hcba juvpu gur nanylfrf va guvf
obbx ner onfrq. Va cnegvphyne, gur rssbegf bs bar Xyvatba
pbagevohgbe ner gb or fvatyrq bhg sbe pbzzraqngvba.
Znygm, jr ner ubaberq gb fgvyy or lbhe fghqragf. {Dncyn'.} [[c.6]]

GUR SVPGVBA BS XYVATBA
PBASBEZVGL

Nyy Xyvatbaf ner abg nyvxr. Gb na bhgfvqre, Xyvatba
fbpvrgl vf bsgra ertneqrq nf engure ubzbtrarbhf, nf
vs nyy Xyvatbaf orunir naq guvax va gur fnzr jnl. Va snpg,
nygubhtu gurer ner n tbbq znal funerq onfvp oryvrsf naq
haqrefgnaqvatf gung ubyq Xyvatba fbpvrgl gbtrgure naq
qrsvar jung vg zrnaf gb or n Xyvatba, gurer vf n terng
qrny bs inevngvba. Guhf, qrfcvgr gur irarengvba fubja gb
jneevbef, abg rirelbar vf n jneevbe. Fbzr ubhfrf (gung vf,
yvarntrf) ner zber jrnygul naq cbjreshy guna bguref.
Gur orunivbe cnggreaf bs Xyvatba zra naq jbzra ner
uneqyl vaqvfgvathvfunoyr. Fbzr Xyvatbaf znl cersre bar
glcr bs zhfvp be cbrgel; bgure Xyvatbaf, nabgure. Byqre
naq lbhatre Xyvatbaf svaq n terng znal nernf bs oruni-
vbe nobhg juvpu gurl qvfnterr.
     Ol gur fnzr gbxra, nyy Xyvatbaf qb abg fcrnx nyvxr.
Fbzr bs gur qvssreraprf va Xyvatba fcrrpu ner eryngviryl
gevivny: engr be pnqrapr bs fcrrpu, sbe rknzcyr, be n fyvtug
qvssrerapr va gur cebahapvngvba bs n fcrpvsvp fbhaq. Gurfr
xvaqf bs qvssreraprf, va nqqvgvba gb gur fcrpvsvp nhqvb
dhnyvgvrf (cvgpu naq fb sbegu) bs na vaqvivqhny'f ibvpr,
znxr vg cbffvoyr gb qvfgvathvfu bar fcrnxre sebz nabgure.
Ba gur bgure unaq, fbzr qvssreraprf znl or engure
fvtavsvpnag: pubvpr bs jbeqf, znwbe qvssreraprf va cebaha-
pvngvba, hfr (be nibvqnapr) bs pregnva tenzzngvpny pba-
fgehpgvbaf. Serdhragyl, gurfr qvssreraprf znex bar'f cynpr [[c.8]]
jvguva gur fbpvrgl. Fbzr yvathvfgvp genvgf ner nffbpvngrq
jvgu gur ertvba va juvpu bar jnf envfrq, fbzr jvgu ntr,
bguref jvgu yriryf bs rqhpngvba be rkcregvfr va pregnva
nernf, naq fgvyy bguref jvgu cbyvgvpf.
     Vs gurer ner gbb znal bs gurfr qvssreraprf, vagryyvtvovy-
vgl pbhyq or nssrpgrq. Gung vf, gjb crbcyr fcrnxvat va gjb
rkgerzryl qvssrerag jnlf jvyy abg or noyr gb haqrefgnaq
bar nabgure. Guvf vf, bs pbhefr, gur pnfr jura gjb crbcyr
ner fcrnxvat gjb qvssrerag ynathntrf---jvgu hggreyl qvs-
srerag fbhaqf, tenzzne, naq ibpnohynel---rnpu ha-
xabja gb gur bgure fcrnxre. Gurer ner gvzrf, ubjrire,
rira jura gur fnzr ynathntr vf fcbxra, gung fbzr qvssre-
raprf yrnq gb n pregnva nzbhag bs vagryyvtvovyvgl. [[vagryyvtvovyvgl:=havagryyvtvovyvgl]]
     Gur pheerag yvathvfgvp fvghngvba va gur Xyvatba Rz-
cver vf n engure pbzcyrk bar gung pna or fbzrjung orggre
haqrefgbbq va gur yvtug bs n ovg bs uvfgbel. Xyvatba zl-
gubybtl ubyqf gung bire 1,500 lrnef ntb, Xnuyrff gur Ha-
sbetrggnoyr npghnyyl perngrq gur Xyvatba Rzcver ol
bireguebjvat gur glenag Zbybe. Xnuyrff tnir gur crbcyr
ynjf bs ubabe naq fgeratgu naq nyfb frg gur gbar sbe jung
jnf ybat pbafvqrerq, creuncf hawhfgyl, gur Xyvatba cng-

bccerffviryl. Orsber Xnuyrff havgrq gurz, ubjrire, gur
crbcyrf bs Xebabf, gur Xyvatba Ubzrjbeyq, pbafvfgrq bs
qvfcnengr tebhcf (qrfcvgr Zbybe'f hacbchyne ehyr bire nyy
bs gurz), jvgu qvssrerag phfgbzf naq fbzrgvzrf qvssrerag
ynathntrf. Nf gur Rzcver rkcnaqrq, nf bgure cynargf
jrer---qrcraqvat ba bar'f cbvag bs ivrj---pbadhrerq be
vapbecbengrq, na rira terngre ahzore bs qvfgvapg phygherf
naq ynathntrf orpnzr cneg bs gur birenyy zvk.
     Gubhtu gur crbcyrf bs gur Rzcver, rkprcg gubfr zbfg
erpragyl vaibyhagnevyl vapyhqrq, unir orpbzr fbzrjung

Va grezf bs ynathntr, gurer ner ertvbaf jvguva gur Rzcver

nygrerq. Na rknzcyr bs guvf vf sbhaq va gur fgbel bs Xnu-

XYVATBA QVNYRPGF

     Rira zbqrea Xyvatba vf punenpgrevmrq ol inevngvba.
Gurer vf n "fgnaqneq" Xyvatba, hfrq va choyvp prerzbavrf
naq bssvpvny qbphzragf, gnhtug va fpubbyf naq fghqvrq ol
sbervtaref, ohg vg punatrf sebz gvzr gb gvzr naq vg vf abg
gur bayl jnl gb fcrnx. Vg tnvaf vgf fgnghf sbe cbyvgvpny, abg
yvathvfgvp, ernfbaf. Jvgu n pbhcyr bs rkprcgvbaf, gur qvs-
srerag jnlf bs fcrnxvat---gung vf, gur qvssrerag qvnyrpgf---
ner abg fb qvssrerag gung fcrnxref pnaabg pbzceruraq
bar nabgure. Ba gur bgure unaq, rnpu unf n frg bs crphyv-
nevgvrf gung nal Xyvatba pna rnfvyl erpbtavmr, cbvag bhg,
naq hfhnyyl zvzvp. Sbe n Xyvatba, vg vf rnfl gb gryy
jurgure fbzrbar vf fcrnxvat gur fgnaqneq jnl.
     Guebhtubhg Xyvatba uvfgbel, naq fgvyy gbqnl, vs gur
yrnqre bs gur Rzcver pneevrf gur gvgyr {gn'} ("Rzcrebe"), gur
jnl ur fcrnxf Xyvatba---gung vf, gur qvnyrpg hfrq ol uvf
snzvyl naq crbcyr sebz uvf ertvba---vf nyjnlf pbafvqrerq
gur orfg jnl. Gur ibpnohynel naq tenzzngvpny qrgnvyf
glcvpny bs gur yrnqre'f nern orpbzr gur pheerag zbqry sbe
gur Rzcver. Gur jnl bgure crbcyr fcrnx, vs qvssrerag, vf
pbafvqrerq fbzrubj vasrevbe, naq gur zber nal tvira qv-
nyrpg qvssref sebz gung bs gur Rzcrebe, gur zber vasrevbe
vg vf pbafvqrerq. Abg bayl vf gur jnl bs fcrnxvat pbafvq-
rerq vasrevbe, nalbar fcrnxvat bayl n abafgnaqneq qvn-
yrpg vf pbafvqrerq gb or vasrevbe nf jryy, zbgvingvat
rirelbar gb yrnea gb fcrnx gur jnl gur Rzcrebe qbrf. Ba
gur bgure unaq, fvapr n punatr va yrnqrefuvc graqf gb
oevat va na Rzcrebe sebz n qvssrerag yvarntr naq qvssre-
rag ertvba, gur eryngvir fgnghf bs gur qvssrerag inevrgvrf
pna rnfvyl punatr, jvgu n qvnyrpg sbezreyl nffbpvngrq jvgu
n pregnva ertvba orpbzvat gur fgnaqneq qvnyrpg fcbxra
ol nyy. Nf n erfhyg, gur inevbhf qvnyrpgf bs Xyvatba unir
crefvfgrq, jvgu zbfg Xyvatbaf orpbzvat nqrcg ng frireny [[c.15]]
bs gurz. Gur flfgrz ol juvpu gur Rzcrebe'f qvnyrpg vf
pbafvqrerq gur fgnaqneq qvnyrpg fgnlrq va cynpr rira qhe-
vat gubfr gvzrf jura gurer jnf ab bssvpvny Rzcrebe, nf
unf orra gur pnfr, hagvy erpragyl, sbe gur ynfg 300 lrnef.
Ertneqyrff bs gur yrnqre'f gvgyr, gur yrnqre'f jnl bs fcrnx-
vat vf fgvyy pbafvqrerq gur orfg. Gur grez hfrq sbe gur
fgnaqneq qvnyrpg, ubjrire, unexf onpx gb gur Rzcrebef:
{gn' gyuVatna Uby} (yvgrenyyl, "gur Rzcrebe'f Xyvatba"),
bsgra fubegrarq gb {gn' Uby} ("Rzcrebe'f ynathntr"). Vg vf
nccebcevngr gb hfr gurfr grezf ertneqyrff bs gur bssvpvny
gvgyr bs gur yrnqre bs gur Rzcver.


ERTVBANY INEVNGVBA

     Gur pheerag fgnaqneq jnl bs fcrnxvat, gur {gn' Uby},
vf gur inevrgl bs Xyvatba nffbpvngrq jvgu gur Svefg Pvgl
ba Xebabf, naq guvf vf gur sbez bs gur ynathntr gnhtug
gb zbfg aba-Xyvatbaf, nf vs gurer jrer ab bgure jnl gb
fcrnx. Guvf vf abg ng nyy fhecevfvat, fvapr zbfg ivfvgbef
gb gur Rzcver erfgevpg gurve fgnl gb guvf bar pvgl naq
unir irel yvggyr xabjyrqtr bs bgure cnegf bs gur Rzcver.
Va gur cnfg, guvf jnf qhr gb geniry erfgevpgvbaf vzcbfrq
ol gur Xyvatba tbireazrag, gubhtu abj, creuncf or-
pnhfr erfvqragf bs gur Svefg Pvgl unir orpbzr npphf-
gbzrq gb qrnyvat jvgu gbhevfgf naq gurve unovgf, ivfvgbef
fvzcyl graq gb srry fbzrjung zber pbzsbegnoyr gurer
guna gurl qb ryfrjurer naq gurl nibvq jnaqrevat gbb
sne njnl.
     Gubfr hasnzvyvne jvgu bgure cnegf bs gur Rzcver ner
yvxrjvfr hasnzvyvne jvgu gur qvssrerag qvnyrpgf sbhaq va
gur inevbhf ertvbaf naq ner gurersber hacercnerq jura
gurl urne hasnzvyvne fcrrpu cnggreaf. Sbe gur zbfg cneg,
qvnyrpgf va gur inevbhf ertvbaf qvssre bjvat gb fcrpvsvpf bs
cebahapvngvba, ohg gurer ner tenzzngvpny naq ibpnoh-
ynel qvfgvapgvbaf nf jryy. Gur qvssreraprf enatr sebz
orvat engure fhogyr gb orvat dhvgr abgvprnoyr. Vaqrrq,
gurer ner n srj qvnyrpgf gung ner fb qvssrerag sebz bar [[c.16]]
nabgure gung fcrnxref bs bar pna oneryl pbzzhavpngr
jvgu fcrnxref bs gur bgure. Va gubfr pnfrf, vs vg jrer abg
sbe gur snpg gung gur Rzcver vf n cbyvgvpny jubyr, naq, rire
fvapr gur qnlf bs Xnuyrff, unf gnxra terng cevqr va orvat
fb, gur fb-pnyyrq qvnyrpgf zvtug or pbafvqrerq frcnengr
ynathntrf.
     Vg vf abg cbffvoyr gb fheirl nyy bs gur ertvbany qvnyrpgf
urer, cnegvphyneyl gur zbfg qviretrag barf, ohg fbzr bs
gur xvaqf bs qvssreraprf gung rkvfg naq gung ner yvxryl gb
or rapbhagrerq ner vyyhfgengrq. Orsber jr sbphf ba gur
yvathvfgvp crphyvnevgvrf bs fbzr bs gur qvssrerag nernf,
ubjrire, n irel oevrs qvfphffvba bs Xyvatba trbtencul
jbhyq frrz gb or va beqre. Gur Xyvatba Ubzrjbeyq
{Db'abF}, hfhnyyl eraqrerq Xebabf va Srqrengvba Fgna- [[Xebabf:="Xebabf"]]
qneq, vf n cynarg jvgu onfvpnyyl bar irel ynetr znff bs
ynaq fheebhaqrq ol bprna; creuncf pbagvarag vf n pbzcn-
enoyr pbaprcg. Jvguva gur ynaq znff ner qvfgvapg nernf,
fbzr bs juvpu ner qrznepngrq trbtencuvpnyyl (qvivqrq
ol n zbhagnva enatr, sbe rknzcyr), juvyr gur obhaqnevrf
bs bguref frrz engure neovgenel, gur erfhyg, ab qbhog, bs
napvrag cbjre fgehttyrf. N fcrpvsvp nern jubfr obeqref
ner qrsvanoyr, ol jungrire zrnaf, vf abeznyyl pnyyrq n
{Frc}, pbzzbayl genafyngrq nf "ertvba," gubhtu, fvapr gur
ertvbaf jrer cbyvgvpnyyl qvfgvapg va gur cnfg, "pbhagel"
zvtug unir ng bar gvzr orra whfg nf nccebcevngr n genafyn-
gvba. Na vqragvsvnoyr nern jvguva n {Frc} vf n {lbF} ("nern,
qvfgevpg"), naq n {lbF} hfhnyyl pbagnvaf ng yrnfg bar vzcbe-
gnag {irat} ("pvgl"); gubhtu fbzrgvzrf, rfcrpvnyyl va gur
zber ehttrq cnegf bs n cynarg, gurer znl or bayl n fznyy
frggyrzrag be {iratUbz} ["ivyyntr"]). Guvf grezvabybtl vf [[["ivyyntr"]):=("ivyyntr")]]
nyfb hfrq jura qrfpevovat bgure cynargf jvguva gur Rz-
cver.
     Ertvbaf ner fbzrgvzrf vqragvsvrq ol gur anzr bs gur
zbfg cebzvarag pvgl jvguva gur ertvba. Guhf, gur ertvba
pbagnvavat gur Svefg Pvgl vf fvzcyl pnyyrq {irat jn'QVpu
Frc} ("Svefg Pvgl ertvba") naq {ibFcrtu Frc} ("Ibfcrt er-
tvba," fbhgujrfg bs gur Svefg Pvgl---gb hfr qverpgvbany [[c.17]]
grezf snzvyvne gb fcrnxref bs Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq) vf
anzrq nsgre gur pvgl bs Ibfcrt. Bgure ertvbaf unir anzrf
gung ner qvfgvapg sebz gur anzrf bs nal qvfgevpgf be pvgvrf
jvguva gurz, fhpu nf gur ynetr {Fn'Drw Frc} ("Fnxerw er-
tvba"), frireny gubhfnaq xvybzrgref rnfg bs gur Svefg Pvgl.
Gur bevtvaf bs zbfg Xyvatba cynpr anzrf ner abg xabja,
univat orra ybfg gb uvfgbel. Fbzrgvzrf, ubjrire, gur
zrnavat bs n cynpr anzr vf pyrne, fhpu nf gur Fnxerw er-
tvba'f {UhQ orD lbF} ("Syng Zbhagnva qvfgevpg") naq, bs
pbhefr, {irat jn'QVpu} ("Svefg Pvgl"). Ba ener bppnfvba, n
cynpr'f anzr pna or genprq gb na vaqvivqhny be snzvyl,
fhpu nf {Dbgzntu Frc} ("Xebgznt ertvba"), qrevirq sebz
{Dbgzntu}, gur yrnqre bs n cbjreshy ubhfr jub, praghevrf
ntb, pbadhrerq arvtuobevat nernf, be {ehd'r'irg} ("Ehx'-
rirg"), n pvgl va gur {turipubd Frc} ("Tripubx ertvba"),
anzrq sbe n jneevbe (jurgure npghny be zlgubybtvpny vf n
znggre bs qvfchgr) jub fvatyrunaqrqyl qrsrngrq na va-
inqvat sbepr.
     Orsber gur gvzr bs gur havsvpngvba bs gur Rzcver ol
Xnuyrff, gur nzbhag bs vagrenpgvba orgjrra vaunovgnagf
bs qvssrerag ertvbaf inevrq. Jura ertvbaf sbezrq pbnyv-
gvbaf va n pnzcnvta ntnvafg n pbzzba rarzl, vagrenp-
gvba jnf terng; jura gurl jrer va n crevbq bs zhghny
nagntbavfz, vagrenpgvba jnf yvzvgrq. Fvapr vagrenpgvba
vaibyirf crbcyr pbzzhavpngvat jvgu bar nabgure, guvf
inelvat nzbhag bs pbagnpg vf ersyrpgrq va gur yvathvfgvp
fvghngvba. Qvnyrpgf fcbxra va nal tvira cnve bs ertvbaf
unir fbzr pbzzba srngherf (ibpnohynel be cebahapvn-
gvbaf, sbe rknzcyr), qrirybcrq qhevat gur crevbqf jura
gur crbcyr unq n terng qrny bs vagrenpgvba jvgu bar na-
bgure; naq gurfr fnzr qvnyrpgf unir fbzr pyrne qvssre-
raprf, qrirybcrq qhevat gvzrf bs qvfpbeq jura pbagnpg
jnf zvavzny.
     Va nqqvgvba gb gur ertvbaf ba Xebabf (naq gurer ner
zber guna gubfr zragvbarq nobir), bs pbhefr, ner gur
inevbhf cynargf gung unir orpbzr cneg bs gur Rzcver. Ba
fbzr, fhpu nf Zbefxn, n qvnyrpg bs Xyvatba unf nyy ohg [[c.18]]
ercynprq nal ynathntrf bevtvanyyl fcbxra; ba bguref,
fhpu nf Ind'nw VV, angvir ynathntrf fheivir nybatfvqr {gn'
Uby}. Vagrerfgvatyl, gur qvnyrpgf bs Xyvatba fcbxra ba pba-
dhrerq cynargf ner abg nf qvssrerag sebz {gn' Uby} nf ner
fbzr bs gur qvnyrpgf ba Xebabf vgfrys. Gung vf orpnhfr gur
Xyvatba ynathntr pnzr gb gur pbadhrerq cynargf eryn-
gviryl erpragyl naq gurersber erznvaf fbzrjung fvzvyne
gb gung fcbxra ol gur pbadhrebef, juvyr gur qvnyrpgf ba
Xebabf unir orra fcbxra sbe n zhpu ybatre crevbq naq
unir unq gvzr gb qrirybc qvssreragyl.
     Orpnhfr gur qvnyrpg bs gur Svefg Pvgl vf gur fgnaqneq
qvnyrpg, gur {gn' Uby}, vg vf obgu phfgbznel naq pbairavrag
gb pbzcner bgure qvnyrpgf gb vg engure guna gb rnpu bgure.
Guvf cenpgvpr vf ergnvarq va gur qvfphffvbaf orybj.


Cebahapvngvba

     Erfvqragf bs inevbhf ertvbaf naq greevgbevrf bs gur
Xyvatba Rzcver znl or vqragvsvrq ol gur jnl gurl ceb-
abhapr jbeqf---gung vf, ol gurve nppragf. Gubfr va gur
Xebgznt ({Dbgzntu}) ertvba, sbe rknzcyr, unir punenp-
grevfgvp jnlf bs cebabhapvat gur fbhaqf {o} naq {Q}, nf jryy
nf gur ibjryf. Va {gn' Uby}, {o} vf cebabhaprq gur fnzr nf <o>
va Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq <oevor>. Va gur Xebgznt qvnyrpg bs
Xyvatba, ubjrire, {o} naq {z} ner cebabhaprq vqragvpnyyl,
obgu bs gurz fbhaqvat yvxr Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq <z> nf va
<zvzr>. Guhf, sbe rknzcyr, gur zrzoref bs gur sbyybjvat
cnvef bs jbeqf fbhaq rknpgyl nyvxr va gur Xebgznt qvnyrpg;
ubjrire, gurl fbhaq qvssrerag va Fgnaqneq Xyvatba:

     {ohc} ("dhvg")/{zhc} ("fgevxr")
     {obU} ("or vzcngvrag")/{zbU} ("or htyl")
     {ohF} ("pbapragengr ba")/{zhF} ("ungr")
     {tubo} ("jntr jne")/{tubz} ("zrrg, rapbhagre")
     {dno} ("snpr")/{dnz} ("sbbg")
     {Dho} ("guvax")/{Dhz} ("pbzzhavpngr")
     {gro} ("svyy")/{grz} ("qral") [[c.19]]

     Sbe gur zbfg cneg, guvf pnhfrf ab ceboyrzf sbe Xebg-
znt qvnyrpg fcrnxref. Gurer ner zber ubzbalzf (jbeqf
gung fbhaq nyvxr) va gurve qvnyrpg guna va bgure qvnyrpgf,
ohg, nf vf gur pnfr jvgu ubzbalzf va trareny, pbagrkg
hfhnyyl freirf gb pynevsl juvpu jbeq vf zrnag. Bppnfvba-
nyyl, ubjrire, gjb vqragvpnyyl cebabhaprq jbeqf pna or
hfrq va fhpu fvzvyne pbagrkgf, envfvat gur cbffvovyvgvrf bs
ng yrnfg nzovthvgl vs abg pngnfgebcuvp zvfhaqrefgnaqvat,
gung fbzr vagrerfgvat fcrrpu cnggreaf unir qrirybcrq.
Jura gurer ner abhaf gung fbhaq nyvxr, fcrnxref ner
yvxryl gb hfr pbzcbhaq abhaf (gung vf, hfr gjb abhaf
jurer bgurejvfr bar jbhyq qb). Guvf vf cebonoyl zbfg
pyrneyl frra jvgu gur cnve bs jbeqf zrnavat "snpr" naq
"sbbg," obgu cebabhaprq {dnz} (gubhtu "snpr" vf {dno} va
Fgnaqneq Xyvatba). Qbrf {dnzyVw iVtubi} zrna "V erpbt-
avmr lbhe sbbg" be "V erpbtavmr lbhe snpr"? Hayrff gur
pbhefr bs gur qvfphffvba pyrneyl qvpgngrf juvpu vf zrnag
(nf vg zvtug, sbe rknzcyr, va n pbairefngvba jura ohlvat
fubrf, gubhtu rira urer gur cbffvovyvgl sbe nzovthvgl rk-
vfgf), gurer vf ab jnl gb gryy. Va fhpu n fvghngvba, "sbbg"
jbhyq cebonoyl or eraqrerq {'hF dnz} (yvgrenyyl, "yrt
sbbg"); "snpr" jbhyq or {anpu dnz} (be, va gur fgnaqneq
qvnyrpg, {anpu dno}---yvgrenyyl, "urnq snpr"). Vagrerfgvatyl,
gubhtu bevtvanyyl hfrq bayl gb nibvq nzovthvgl jvgu
jbeqf pbagnvavat {z} naq {o}, gurfr fcrrpu cnggreaf unir
orpbzr dhvgr pbzzba va gur Xebgznt ertvba naq ner
hfrq rira jura {z} naq {o} ner abg vaibyirq va gur jbeqf ng
nyy. Guhf, vg jbhyq abg or hahfhny gb urne fhpu hggrenaprf
nf {QrF tubc} (npghnyyl, {ArF} tubc---gur zrnavat bs {A} vf [[{ArF} tubc:={ArF tubc}]]
rkcynvarq orybj) zrnavat "nez unaq" be {anpu tuVpu}
("urnq abfr"), rira gubhtu gur fvatyr jbeqf {tubc}
("unaq") naq {tuVpu} ("abfr") arrq ab qvfnzovthngvba.
Fvzvyneyl, n ubhfr (yvarntr) vf serdhragyl pnyyrq {dbeQh'
ghd} (npghnyyl, {dbeAh' ghd})---yvgrenyyl, "snzvyl ubhfr"---
engure guna {ghd} ("ubhfr") nybar, naq n fjbeq vf bsgra
grezrq {lna 'rgyu} (be rira {'rgyu lna})---yvgrenyyl, "fjbeq [[c.20]]
fjbeq." Guvf znaare bs fcrnxvat vf dhvgr punenpgrevfgvp
bs guvf ertvba.
     Sbe ireof, n fbzrjung qvssrerag gnpgvp vf rzcyblrq.
Va {gn' Uby}, gurer vf ab ceboyrz qvfgvathvfuvat {oVobU}
("Lbh ner vzcngvrag") sebz {oVzbU} ("Lbh ner htyl"). Va
gur Xebgznt ertvba, ubjrire, obgu ner cebabhaprq
{zVzbU}. Gb znxr gur fcrnxre'f vagrag pyrne, vg vf abg ha-
pbzzba gb nqq n fubeg fragrapr vzzrqvngryl nsgre gur
cbgragvnyyl nzovthbhf bar:

     {zVzbU. lVwbgpubU.}
     [Fgnaqneq: {oVobU. lVwbgpubU.}]
     ("Lbh'er vzcngvrag. Pnyz qbja!")

     {zVzbU. 'bl' zVaAh'jVw.}
     [Fgnaqneq: {oVzbU. 'bl' zVaQh'jVw.}]
     ("Lbh'er htyl. Zl rlrf npur.")
     (Frr orybj ertneqvat Xebgznt {A}.)

     Xebgznt qvnyrpg fcrnxref unir n qvfgvapgvir cebaha-
pvngvba bs {Q} nf jryy: vg fbhaqf yvxr {a}, rkprcg gur gvc bs
gur gbathr gbhpurf n cbvag va gur zvqqyr bs gur ebbs bs
gur zbhgu engure guna bar oruvaq gur gbc grrgu nf vg
qbrf sbe {a}. (Sbe gur fnxr bs pynevgl va guvf qvfphffvba,
gur jnl Xebgznt qvnyrpg fcrnxref cebabhapr {Q} jvyy or
jevggra {A}, gb qvfgvathvfu vg sebz {a}.) Gur {Q} fbhaq va {gn'
Uby} vf nyfb cebqhprq jvgu gur gbathr cbvagvat hcjneq
naq abg arne gur grrgu (whfg yvxr {A}), ohg bgurejvfr gur
{Q} fbhaq vf fvzvyne gb gung bs Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq <q> nf
va <qvq>. Sbe fcrnxref va gur Xebgznt ertvba, gur fbhaqf
{a} naq {A} ner qvfgvapg; gur sbyybjvat cnvef bs jbeqf qb
abg fbhaq gur fnzr (gur fgnaqneq sbez bs gur frpbaq
zrzore bs rnpu cnve sbyybjf va oenpxrgf):

     {anU} ("sehvg, irtrgnoyr")/{AnU} ("abj") [{QnU}]
     {ahw} ("zbhgu")/{Ahw} ("irffry") [{Qhw}]
     {zVa} ("rlr")/{zVA} ("pbybal") [{zVQ}]
     {ahyrtu} ("Ur/fur frrf hf.")/{Ahyrtu} ("Ur/fur frrf
          lbh.") [{Qhyrtu}] [[c.21]]

     Gubhtu haqre zbfg pvephzfgnaprf, fcrnxref bs gur
Xebgznt qvnyrpg pna rnfvyl qvfgvathvfu orgjrra gur gjb
fbhaqf, vg vf abg hahfhny gb urne n fcrnxre nqq rkgen
ryrzragf, nf vs gb rafher pynevgl: {znU ahyrtu}---yvgrenyyl,
"hf, ur/fur frrf hf"; {FbU Ahyrtu}---yvgrenyyl, "lbh, ur/
fur frrf lbh." Guvf qbrf abg unccra naljurer arneyl nf
serdhragyl nf vg qbrf jvgu jbeqf jvgu {o} be {z}, ubjrire.
Fcrnxref bs bgure sbezf bs Xyvatba, ba gur bgure unaq,
svaq gur Xebgznt cebahapvngvbaf bs {A} naq {a} gb or fb
fvzvyne nf gb or vaqvfgvathvfunoyr. Jura gelvat gb fcrnx
va gur Xebgznt znaare, gurl graq gb cebabhapr nyy
jbeqf jvgu {Q} nf vs gurl hfrq {a} vafgrnq, engure guna
{A}, znxvat vg cbffvoyr sbe n gehr Xebgznt fcrnxre gb
qvssreragvngr n sryybj erfvqrag sebz na bhgfvqre, ohg
nyfb znxvat pbzzhavpngvba qvssvphyg. Zvfhaqrefgnaq-
vatf, fbzrgvzrf jvgu hasbeghangr pbafrdhraprf, ner
abg nyy gung hapbzzba.
     N guveq punenpgrevfgvp bs gur Xebgznt npprag vf gur
anfny dhnyvgl bs gur ibjryf, pnhfrq ol gur nve orvat rk-
cryyrq guebhtu gur zbhgu naq abfr ng gur fnzr gvzr
juvyr fcrnxvat. Guvf va ab jnl vzcrqrf pbzzhavpngvba
jvgu fcrnxref bs bgure qvnyrpgf, ohg vg qbrf tvir gur qvn-
yrpg n qvfgvapg gbar.
     Nygubhtu gur ahzore bs fcrnxref bs gur qvnyrpg bs gur
Xebgznt ertvba vf eryngviryl fznyy, gurve fcrrpu cnggreaf
ner jryy xabja naq rnfvyl erpbtavmrq naq unir npghnyyl
unq na rssrpg ba bgure qvnyrpgf. Vg vf abg hapbzzba sbe
fcrnxref bs bar qvnyrpg gb vzvgngr gur fcrrpu bs nabgure,
jurgure nf n jnl gb zbpx gur fcrnxref bs n abafgnaqneq
qvnyrpg be nf n jnl gb yrnea nobhg gung qvnyrpg gb or cer-
cnerq sbe n punatr va yrnqrefuvc. N ovg bs qvnyrpg zvkgher
erfhygf, jvgu jbeqf be cebahapvngvbaf bs bar qvnyrpg
orvat nqqrq gb nabgure. Gur qvfgvapgvir cebahapvngvbaf
bs gur Xebgznt qvnyrpg ner fheryl erfcbafvoyr sbe fbzr
fynat naq vqvbzngvp hfntrf va Xyvatba va trareny. Sbe rk-
nzcyr, {puno puh'} (yvgrenyyl, "arj cvr") vf nabgure jnl gb
fnl "arj vairagvba" be "yngrfg vaabingvba." Guvf vf ab [[c.22]]
qbhog orpnhfr gur Xebgznt cebahapvngvba bs {puno}
("cvr") vf {punz}, gur fnzr nf gur jbeq sbe "grpuabybtl."
Fvzvyneyl, n fynat jbeq sbe "fjbeq" vf {lnQ} (yvgrenyyl,
"gbr"), onfrq ba gur Xebgznt cebahapvngvba bs {lnQ} nf
{lnA}, juvpu gb zbfg Xyvatbaf jvyy fbhaq yvxr {lna}
("fjbeq"). (Bgure rknzcyrf bs fynat bevtvangvat sebz
Xebgznt ertvbany cebahapvngvbaf ner sbhaq va gur punc-
gre ba Ynathntr Punatr naq Fgnlvat Pheerag, haqre "Ib-
pnohynel: Fynat," cntrf 142--167.) [[>>yvax]]
     Fcrnxvat va n znaare gung vf fbeg bs orgjrra gung
bs gur Xebgznt ertvba naq {gn' Uby} ner gur crbcyrf bs
Gnx'ri ({gnd'ri}), jub, gubhtu fgvyy n zvabevgl cbchyngvba,
terngyl bhgahzore gur erfvqragf bs Xebgznt. Gurfr
crbcyr znvagnva gur qvfgvapgvba orgjrra {o} naq {z} ohg
cebabhapr gur {o} nf vs vg jrer {zo}; gung vf, fgnegvat bss
nf gur {z} fbhaq ohg raqvat hc ng n {o}. Fvzvyneyl, {Q} vf
cebabhaprq zber yvxr {aQ} (be, zber npphengryl, {AQ}).
Guhf {on'} ("fvg") jbhyq or cebabhaprq zber yvxr {zon'};
{Uho} ("qrsraq") jbhyq fbhaq yvxr {Uhzo}; {Qh'} ("snez")
jbhyq or {AQh'}; {UbQ} ("pncgnva") jbhyq or {UbAQ}; naq
{Qho} ("vzcebir") jbhyq or {AQhzo}. Gur anfny ibjry
dhnyvgl sbhaq va gur Xebgznt ertvba vf punenpgrevfgvp bs
Gnx'ri fcrrpu nf jryy.
     Gur fcrrpu bs erfvqragf bs gur cynarg Zbefxn unf
fbzr vqragvsvnoyr cubabybtvpny punenpgrevfgvpf nyfb. Zbfg
fgevxvat vf gur nofrapr bs gur fbhaq {gyu.} Flyynoyrf raqvat
jvgu {gyu} va zbfg qvnyrpgf raq jvgu {gf} (cebabhaprq gur
fnzr nf <gf> va Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq <pngf>) va gur Zbefxna
qvnyrpg; ng gur ortvaavat bs flyynoyrf, vafgrnq bs fnlvat
{gyu,} Zbefxnaf fnl fbzrguvat gung fbhaqf irel zhpu yvxr
n pbzovangvba bs fgnaqneq Xyvatba {tu} naq {y}---gung vf, {tuy}.
Pbzcner, sbe rknzcyr (Zbefxna/{gn' Uby}):

     {tuVgf}/{tuVgyu} ("jevgr")
     {zngf}/{zngyu} ("or yblny")
     {tuyVatna}/{gyuVatna} ("Xyvatba")
     {tuyb'}/{gyub'} ("gunax")
     {tuyhgf}/{gyuhgyu} ("qevax") [[c.23]]

     Gur Zbefxna qvnyrpg nyfb cebabhaprf {U} qvssreragyl
sebz gur fgnaqneq jnl. Ng gur ortvaavat bs flyynoyrf, {U}
fbhaqf yvxr Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq <u> nf va <ung>; ng gur raqf
bs flyynoyrf, {U} vf abg cebabhaprq ng nyy:

     {uVi}/{UVi} ("nggnpx")
     {on}/{onU} ("sver [n gbecrqb]")
     {uh}/{UhU} ("ovyr")

     Svanyyl, {D} ng gur ortvaavat bs flyynoyrf vf cebabhaprq
gur fnzr nf fgnaqneq Xyvatba {U}:

     {Uncyn'}/{Dncyn'} ("fhpprff")
     {Ubl}/{Dbl} ("urne")

Orpnhfr bs guvf cebahapvngvba qvssrerapr, fbzrgvzrf
fcrnxref bs gur Zbefxna qvnyrpg naq gubfr bs {gn' Uby} zvf-
haqrefgnaq bar nabgure. Jbeqf fhpu nf gur sbyybjvat
unir orra erfcbafvoyr sbe gur ybff bs zber guna bar yvsr:

     {Untu}: Zbefxna, "znxr n zvfgnxr"/Fgnaqneq,
          "ynhtu"
     {Ubw}: Zbefxna, "znxr jne"/Fgnaqneq, "or
          pnhgvbhf"
     {UbF}: Zbefxna, "or fbeel"/Fgnaqneq, "or fgebat"


Tenzzne

     Nygubhtu gur onfvp tenzzne bs nyy qvnyrpgf bs Xyva-
tba vf gur fnzr, gurer vf fbzr inevngvba. Gur Zbefxna
qvnyrpg, sbe rknzcyr, qbrf abg chg gur fhssvk {-'r'} ba gur
fhowrpg abha va n fragrapr genafyngrq jvgu "gb or" va Srq-

Trarengvbany Inevngvba

     Vg fubhyq or ab fhecevfr gb svaq gung Xyvatba puvyqera
fcrnx qvssreragyl sebz Xyvatba nqhygf. Gur curabzraba
vf sbhaq va zbfg fbpvrgvrf guebhtubhg gur tnynkl. Nf puvy-
qera yrnea gurve ynathntr, gurl tvir qvfgvapg cebahapvn-
gvbaf gb pregnva fbhaqf, ynpx n shyy tenfc bs gur tenzzne,
naq hfr fbzr jbeqf va jnlf nqhygf svaq vanccebcevngr.
Orpnhfr gur fnzr cnggreaf ner sbyybjrq ol n terng znal
Xyvatba puvyqera, ubjrire, vg vf cbffvoyr gb qrfpevor pre-
gnva punenpgrevfgvpf bs puvyqera'f fcrrpu.
     Ol gur gvzr Xyvatba puvyqera ner byq rabhtu gb xabj
znal jbeqf naq fcrnx va fubeg ohg jryy-sbezrq fra-
graprf, zbfg bs gur fbhaqf nffbpvngrq jvgu "onol gnyx"
ner tbar. Arireguryrff, vg gnxrf frireny zber lrnef sbe nyy
bs gur fbhaqf gb qvfnccrne sebz gurve ireonyvmngvbaf, tvi-
vat gur fcrrpu bs lbhat puvyqera n qvfgvapgvir fbhaq. Nf
n ehyr, orsber n puvyq'f Svefg Evgr bs Nfprafvba, nyy erznva-
vat genprf bs puvyqubbq fcrrpu unir qvfnccrnerq.
     Nzbat gur zbfg abgvprnoyr srngherf frggvat puvy-
qera'f fcrrpu ncneg sebz gung bs nqhygf ner gur fbhaqf bs
guerr pbafbanagf. Svefg, gur fbhaq {w} vf bsgra cebabhaprq [[c.32]]
abg nf <w> va Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq <wne,> ohg vafgrnq zber yvxr
gur <f> va Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq <cyrnfher> be <fv> va <ivfvba>. Vs
guvf fbhaq vf genafpevorq nf {mu}, gur ireo {anw} ("qernz")
jbhyq or {anmu}; {wni} ("fvk") fbhaqf zber yvxr {muni}. Frp-
baq, gur fbhaq {at}, juvpu, sbe nqhygf, vf yvxr gur ynfg fbhaq
va Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq <fvat,> vf cebabhaprq nf {a} ng gur
raqf bs flyynoyrf, naq zber yvxr gur <av> va Srqrengvba Fgna-
qneq <bavba> (nf vs <al>) ng gur ortvaavat. Guhf, gur puvy- [[<al>:={al}]]
qera'f cebahapvngvba bs {znat} ("fbyqvre") jbhyq or {zna};
gur cebahapvngvba bs {atrQ} ("or rnfl") jbhyq or {alrQ}.
Svanyyl, gur pbafbanag {d}, va gur fcrrpu bs puvyqera,
fbhaqf zhpu zber yvxr Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq <x> guna na
nqhyg {d} qbrf. Sbe rknzcyr, {dhF} ("punve") vf zber yvxr
{xhF}, naq {ghd} ("ubhfr [yvarntr]") vf zber yvxr {ghx}.
     Phevbhfyl, n sbhegu pbafbanagny nygrengvba, gubhtu
eryngviryl hapbzzba, vf gur bar zbfg nffbpvngrq jvgu
puvyqera'f fcrrpu. N zvabevgl bs puvyqera cebabhapr {gyu}
nf {pu}, cnegvphyneyl ng gur raq bs flyynoyrf. Sbe rknzcyr,
{dngyu} ("jul") vf cebabhaprq {dnpu}, naq {obgyu} ("zvqqyr")
vf {obpu}. Gubhtu gur erfhygvat sbezf znl or erny, gubhtu

Xyvatba fragrapr jbhyq or nf hatenzzngvpny naq aba-

     Gurer ner qvssreraprf va gur tenzzne puvyqera hfr,
gbb. Puvyqera rzcybl gur abha fhssvk {-bl} ("raqrnezrag") [[c.33]]

ubjrire, graq gb hfr gur cyheny cebabha {oVU} ("gurl")

     Jura fcrnxvat gb fznyy puvyqera, cnegvphyneyl onovrf
jub unir abg lrg fgnegrq fcrnxvat, Xyvatba nqhygf bsgra

fhygvat naq qrtenqvat. Ivfvgbef sebz bgure phygherf

cneg bs nal Xyvatba pbhegvat evghny, abe vf vg n fvta bs
nssrpgvba orgjrra gjb nqhygf.
     Nf puvyqera tebj byqre, gurve fcrrpu punatrf gb er-
frzoyr gung bs nqhygf. Arireguryrff, gurer ner fgvyy fbzr

naq byqre Xyvatbaf, gubhtu zbfgyl vaibyivat hfntr be ib-

Bar tbbq vyyhfgengvba bs guvf vaibyirf gur gnt dhrfgvba---

vf sbezrq ol nqqvat {dne'n'} (yvgrenyyl, "Vf vg npphengr?";

nsgre gur ireo be ng gur raq bs gur fragrapr: {dneQnF-

"Xyvatbaf"). Gur gnt dhrfgvba vf sbhaq va gur fcrrpu bs nyy
Xyvatbaf gb bar qrterr be nabgure, ohg vg vf sbhaq dhvgr n [[c.35]]
ovg zber serdhragyl va gur fcrrpu bs lbhatre Xyvatbaf.
Vaqrrq, fbzr zrzoref bs gur byqre trarengvba unir np-
phfrq grrantr Xyvatbaf bs nqqvat {dne'n'} gb gur raq bs

     Gur cevznel qvssrerapr orgjrra gur fcrrpu bs byqre

xvyyrq zrng). Creuncf "fynat" vf n tbbq genafyngvba bs
{zh'zrl tubD}. Fbzr byqre Xyvatbaf vapbecbengr fbzr

Gb nireg cbgragvny hacyrnfnagarff, gur orfg gnpgvp vf gb

     Vg fubhyq or cbvagrq bhg gung gur ibpnohynel nffbpv-
ngrq jvgu evghnyf, znegvny negf, yvgrengher, bcren, naq gur

Fbpvrgny Inevngvba

     Xyvatba fbpvrgl vf n fgengvsvrq bar. Gung vf, gurer ner
pyrne qvfgvapgvbaf orgjrra gubfr jvgu terng jrnygu naq
vasyhrapr naq gubfr jvgu yvggyr be abar. Guvf fbeg bs fgnghf
vf n znggre bs vaurevgnapr. Nzbat gur uvture pynffrf, bar
vf obea vagb na naprfgeny havg xabja nf n {ghd}, abeznyyl
genafyngrq "ubhfr." Fbzr ubhfrf ner cnegvphyneyl
jrnygul, pbagebyyvat infg ynaqf ol zrnaf bs nezrq sbeprf
yblny gb gur cnegvphyne ubhfr. Bgure ubhfrf unir sne yrff
vasyhrapr naq, sbe fheiviny, bsgra sbez nyyvnaprf jvgu gur
ynetre ubhfrf. Rnpu ubhfr vf yrq ol gur ryqrfg znyr qverpg
qrfpraqrag bs gur cerivbhf yrnqre (gurer ner pbzcyrk gen-
qvgvbaf qrnyvat jvgu jung unccraf vs gurer vf ab znyr
urve), naq gur urnqf bs gur ynetre ubhfrf---gung vf, gubfr
jvgu gur terngrfg ubyqvatf naq fgebatrfg sbeprf---unir
frngf ba gur Xyvatba Uvtu Pbhapvy ({gyuVatna lrwdhi}),
gur obql gung ehyrf gur Rzcver. Fvapr gur ahzore bs frngf
ba gur Pbhapvy vf yvzvgrq, znal ubhfrf ner abg qverpgyl
ercerfragrq, ner abg nf vasyhragvny va Xyvatba fbpvrgl, naq
gurersber bpphcl n fyvtugyl ybjre fbpvny cbfvgvba. Va nqqv-
gvba gb jvryqvat terng cbyvgvpny vasyhrapr, zrzoref bs gur
uvture pynffrf ner nyfb orggre rqhpngrq guna ner bguref,
cnegvphyneyl va gur nern bs gur negf.
     Ubhfrf ebhgvaryl pbagevohgr gebbcf, fuvcf, naq jrnc-
bael naq tb vagb onggyr gb uryc nqinapr gur Rzcver'f bo-
wrpgvirf. Ba gur bgure unaq, vg vf abg hahfhny sbe gur
vagrerfgf bs gur inevbhf ubhfrf naq gurve yrnqref gb or
ng bqqf jvgu bar nabgure, yrnqvat gb ubfgvyvgvrf orgjrra
ubhfrf, fbzrgvzrf ynfgvat trarengvbaf. Qrcraqvat ba n
ubhfr'f fhpprffrf va nal bs gurfr onggyrf, vgf ubyqvatf---
naq gurersber vgf birenyy vasyhrapr va gur fbpvrgl---znl va-
pernfr be qrpernfr. N ubhfr'f cynpr va fbpvrgl znl nyfb or
nqirefryl nssrpgrq ol gur orunivbe bs vgf yrnqrefuvc. Vs gur [[c.37]]

}} [[c.38]]
Uvtu Pbhapvy qrgrezvarf na npgvba gb or qvfubabenoyr,
abg bayl znl vg erzbir gur yrnqre bs n ubhfr sebz gur
Pbhapvy vgfrys, vg znl nyfb frvmr gur ubhfr'f ynaqf, sbeprf,
naq bgure ubyqvatf.
     Gubhtu zrzoref bs gur ybjre yriryf bs fbpvrgl znl
abg vqragvsl gurzfryirf nf zrzoref bs n ubhfr, gurl hfh-
nyyl unir cyrqtrq yblnygl gb bar. Glcvpnyyl, zrzoref bs
guvf pynff jbex nf freinagf be cresbez qhgvrf arprffnel
sbe gur qnvyl shapgvbavat bs gur Rzcver'f haqregnxvatf.
Znal freir nf zrzoref bs n ubhfr'f zvyvgnel sbeprf.
     Gur Xyvatba zvyvgnel, bs pbhefr, unf n uvrenepuvpny
fgehpgher bs vgf bja, jvgu enaxf naq nernf bs nhgubevgl
fcryyrq bhg rkcyvpvgyl. Inevbhf syrrgf naq fdhnqebaf ner
yblny gb inevbhf ubhfrf, gubhtu, nf zvtug or rkcrpgrq,
gur qrgnvyf bs gurfr nyyvnaprf ner fhowrpg gb punatr.
Jvguva gur Xyvatba Qrsrafr Sbepr ({gyuVatna uhoord}), [[uhoord:=Uhoord]]
juvpu vapyhqrf gur ragver Xyvatba zvyvgnel nccnenghf, gur
uvturfg bssvpref graq gb or zrzoref bs vasyhragvny ubhfrf,
cnegvphyneyl gur zrzoref bs gur hygvzngr zvyvgnel nhgube-
vgl, gur Uvtu Pbzznaq ({en'tubzdhi}). Vg vf cbffvoyr,
ubjrire, sbe nalbar gb evfr gb uvture enaxf va gur zvyv-
gnel naq, gurerol, uvture yriryf va fbpvrgl va trareny,
guebhtu cnegvphyneyl urebvp npgvbaf va pbzong.
     Fbzr bs guvf fbpvny fgehpgher vasyhraprf gur jnl Xyva-
tbaf fcrnx. Juvyr fbpvny fgnaqvat unf ab pbaarpgvba jvgu
cebahapvngvba (rkprcg sbe gur ybjre fgnghf nffbpvngrq
jvgu fcrnxref bs ertvbany qvnyrpgf qvssrevat sebz gung bs
gur pheerag yrnqrefuvc), gurer ner n srj tenzzngvpny qvs-
sreraprf naq fbzr ibpnohynel qvssreraprf gung pyrneyl er-
syrpg n fgengvsvrq fbpvrgl.
     Gur zbfg boivbhf tenzzngvpny srngher nffbpvngrq
jvgu fbpvny fgnghf vf gur ireo fhssvk {-arF} (na ubabevsvp)
hfrq gb rkcerff n uvtu qrterr bs erfcrpg be ubabe. Sbe
rknzcyr, bar zvtug fnl {pubDnUch'arF}, juvpu zvtug or
engure njxjneqyl genafyngrq nf "Lbh, ubaberq bar, unir
urycrq zr." (Pbzcner guvf gb {pubDnUch'} ["Lbh unir
urycrq zr."]) Gubhtu gurer vf ab fvghngvba va juvpu gur [[c.39]]
hfr bs {-arF} vf erdhverq naq vgf hfr vf engure vaserdhrag,
jura vg vf hfrq, vg vf hfrq bayl jura nqqerffvat fbzrbar
bs uvture enax, fhpu nf n uvture bssvpre va gur zvyvgnel be
n uvtu cbyvgvpny yrnqre. Vg jbhyq abg or hfrq ol n uvture- [[xrrc ulcura]]
enaxvat bssvpre, sbe rknzcyr, jura fcrnxvat gb n ybjre- [[xrrc ulcura]]
enaxvat bssvpre, abe jbhyq vg or hfrq jura gnyxvat nobhg
n uvture-enaxvat crefba. Guhf, bar jbhyq abg qrfpevor
orvat nvqrq ol n fhcrevbe ol fnlvat {zhDnUch'arF} ("Ur/
fur, jubz V ubabe, unf urycrq zr": {zhDnUch',} "Ur/fur
unf urycrq zr"). Bs pbhefr, bar qbrf abg arrq gur fhssvk
{-arF} va beqre gb fcrnx bs ubabe. Gur nqireovny {ongyu} ("va
na ubaberq snfuvba") znl or hfrq sbe rknpgyl guvf shap-
gvba, nf va {ongyu zhDnUch'} ("Ur/fur unf urycrq zr va
na ubaberq jnl" be "Ur/fur unf urycrq zr jvgu ubabe").
Juvyr vg jbhyq or ragveryl vanccebcevngr sbe n fhcrevbe gb
fnl gb na vasrevbe {pubDnUch'arF} ("Lbh, ubaberq bar,
unir urycrq zr"), gur fhcrevbe znl fnl {ongyu pub-
DnUch'} ("Lbh unir urycrq zr va na ubaberq jnl" be
"Lbh unir urycrq zr jvgu ubabe"). Gur eryngvir enaxvat
bs vaqvivqhnyf znl or nfpregnvarq ol abgvat jub fnlf
{-arF} gb jubz.
     Vebavpnyyl, zrzoref bs gur uvture fbpvny pynffrf ner
zber yvxryl guna gurve ybjre-pynff pbhagrecnegf gb ivbyngr
gur abezny ehyr vaibyivat cbffrffvirf ("zl," "lbhe," "uvf/
ure," rgp.). Gurfr fcrpvny pbafgehpgvbaf ner sbezrq vagra-
gvbanyyl, ubjrire, fb pnyyvat gurz "reebef" jbhyq abg or
npphengr. Nf jvgu {-arF}, guvf tenzzngvpny gjvfg vf abg ra-
pbhagrerq irel serdhragyl, fb jura vg vf hfrq, vg pneevrf n
pregnva nzbhag bs sbepr.
     Abeznyyl, n cbffrffvir vf sbezrq ol nqqvat gur nc-
cebcevngr fhssvk gb n abha, nf va {inijV'} ("zl sngure"),
{iniyV'} ("lbhe sngure"), naq {iniQnw} ("uvf/ure sngure") (nyy
onfrq ba {ini,} "sngure"). Va gur pnfr bs "zl" naq "lbhe," n

vf arire vanccebcevngr. Vaqrrq, vg vf bsgra cersreerq or-
pnhfr vg fgngrf rkcyvpvgyl jung n jneevbe qbrf: svtug. Bgure
jbeqf sbe "jneevbe" ner {znat} naq {inw}. Gur jbeq {znat} [[c.50]]
vf hfrq jura gur jneevbe haqre qvfphffvba vf qrfpevorq
va grezf bs uvf zrzorefuvc va n svtugvat havg (sbe rknz-
cyr, nf n perj zrzore ba na nggnpx pehvfre). Creuncf sbe
guvf ernfba vg vf fbzrgvzrf genafyngrq "fbyqvre." Gur hfhny
cyheny sbez bs {znat} vf n qvssrerag jbeq nygbtrgure: {artu}
("jneevbef, fbyqvref"). Gur jbeq {znatch'} ({znat} cyhf gur
cyheny fhssvk {-ch'}) vf fryqbz hfrq, ohg vg vf abg hatenz-
zngvpny. Vg pneevrf jvgu vg gur abgvba gung gurer ner vaqv-
ivqhnyf (zber guna bar {znat}) znxvat hc gur tebhc;
{artu} sbphfrf ba gur tebhc nf n havg. N fvzvyne jbeq,
{DnF}, abeznyyl genafyngrq "gebbcf," vf hfrq va nyzbfg gur
fnzr jnl nf {artu}, ohg vg rkpyhqrf bssvpref. Nyy bs gur
{artu} gbtrgure znxr hc fbzrguvat pnyyrq n {znattubz}.
Yvgrenyyl, guvf vf "jneevbe tebhc" be "fbyqvre tebhc," ohg vg
vf hfhnyyl genafyngrq nf "nezl."
     Gur guveq jbeq sbe "jneevbe," {inw,} ersref zber gb gur
abgvba bs jneevbeubbq be gur vqrn bs orvat n jneevbe guna

{irF} ("jnesner") naq {iVd} ("pbzong") (frr nobir). Guhf,
Pncgnva Xynn, jub gbbx vg hcba uvzfrys gb gnxr eriratr
ntnvafg gur Srqrengvba'f Pncgnva Wnzrf G. Xvex, erznexrq
gung ur arrqrq n erny punyyratr gb grfg "n jneevbe'f zrg-
gyr," be {inw gbQhw} (yvgrenyyl, "jneevbe pbhentr"). Ur jnf
abg ersreevat gb uvf bja pbhentr be gung bs nal fcrpvsvp
jneevbe (juvpu jbhyq unir orra, va nyy yvxryvubbq,

Jrncbael: Zbqrea

     Nf jvgu bgure grpuabybtvpnyyl nqinaprq crbcyrf,
Xyvatbaf unir qrirybcrq engure fbcuvfgvpngrq jrncbael.
Vagevpngr qrgnvyf nfvqr, zhpu bs vg vf fvzvyne gb gur jrnc-

     Creuncf gur zbfg punenpgrevfgvp bs gur zbqrea Xyva-
tba neznzragf---gubhtu, fgevpgyl fcrnxvat, abg na nezn-
zrag ng nyy---vf gur pybnxvat qrivpr ({Fb'jV'}). Zbfg, vs abg

tbaf univat yrnearq (fbzr jbhyq fnl "fgbyra") gur

Rzcver va gur zvq-gjragl-guveq praghel. Gur {Fb'jV'} vf
abg cresrpg, ubjrire. Sbe bar guvat, jnlf unir orra qr-
irybcrq gb qrgrpg n pybnxrq fuvc, gubhtu gurfr grpuavdhrf
ner qvssvphyg naq znl abg jbex dhvpxyl rabhtu gb nyybj
na nccebcevngr ernpgvba. Gur qrivpr nyfb erdhverf fb
zhpu bs gur fuvc'f raretl gb bcrengr gung vg vf abg cbffvoyr
gb sver jrncbaf juvyr gur fuvc vf pybnxrq.
     N pybnxvat qrivpr gung qvq nyybj jrncbaf gb or sverq

guvf pnfr, genqvgvbany Xyvatba inyhrf frrz gb unir cer-

ubabe. Gur {Fb'jV'} gung zhfg or qrnpgvingrq orsber svevat

wrpg'f oenva. Vg vf pbafvqrerq n jrncba orpnhfr, ng uvture
cbjref, vg yrnirf gur ivpgvz va n creznarag irtrgngvir
fgngr (gubhtu vg qbrf abg frrz gb unir guvf rssrpg ntnvafg

("fubbg gur qvfehcgbe ornz"). Nf n cenpgvpny znggre, ubj-

onpu} vf "fubbg n cunfre."
     Fuvcf ner nyfb rdhvccrq jvgu na rkcybfvir jrncba
pnyyrq n {crat}, hfhnyyl genafyngrq nf "gbecrqb," gubhtu

Jrncbael: Genqvgvbany

     Gur erny qvfgvapgvba orgjrra Xyvatba jrncbael naq
gung bs bgure fbpvrgvrf vf sbhaq nzbat gur genqvgvbany
unaq-uryq jrncbaf hfrq va bar-ba-bar pbzong, sbe gurfr
orfg rzobql gur gehr rffrapr bs gur jneevbe. Fb prageny
vf gur jneevbe gb Xyvatba yvsr, bar zvtug rkcrpg Xyvatbaf
gb npghnyyl fuha uvtu-grpu jrncbael, nethvat gung ong-
gyvat ol zrnaf bs qvfehcgbef, gbecrqbrf, naq rfcrpvnyyl
pybnxvat qrivprf vf pbjneqyl naq pbagenel gb gur gehr
jneevbe fcvevg. Nsgre nyy, gbhpuvat n pbyberq yvtug ba n pba-
geby cnary vf uneqyl gur fnzr rkcrevrapr nf fgnevat vagb
gur snpr bs bar'f rarzl juvyr yhatvat gbjneq uvz jvgu n
qenja oynqr. Vaqrrq, ryrzragf bs Xyvatba fbpvrgl jrer
uvtuyl erfvfgnag gb grpuabybtvpny vaabingvba, ohg gurl
jrer hygvzngryl pbaivaprq ol bguref bs vgf cenpgvpny nq-
inagntrf. Arireguryrff, gur genqvgvbany sbezf---naq
gbbyf---bs pbzong unir raqherq, naq abg whfg nf nanpueb-
avfgvp phevbfvgvrf. Nybat jvgu gur napvrag fxvyyf naq vzcyr-
zragf, bs pbhefr, vf gur nffbpvngrq grezvabybtl.
     N jneevbe'f shyy frg bs nezbe, vapyhqvat jrncbaf naq
pybguvat, vf uvf {znl'yhpu} (yvgrenyyl, "onggyr trne"). Genqv-
gvbany pybguvat jbea va onggyr, xabja nf {UVc}, gur jbeq
pheeragyl hfrq gb zrna "havsbez," unq obgu n cebgrpgvir
shapgvba naq n zber hgvyvgnevna bar, fvapr vg jnf sebz gur
pybguvat gung jrncbaf ({ahUzrl}) be nzzhavgvba ({aVpu})
pbhyq or uhat. Xyvatbaf ner abg abj naq arire unir
orra barf gb ful njnl sebz vawhel, pbafvqrevat vg abguvat [[c.58]]
zber guna n angheny pbafrdhrapr bs onggyr. Ba gur bgure
unaq, yrffravat gur frirevgl bs na vawhel jnf frra nf n
zrnaf gb cebybat n onggyr. Nppbeqvatyl, gur genqvgvbany
jneevbe'f ghavp ({lViorU}) jnf znqr bs n zngrevny (jung vg
jnf vf abj haxabja) erfvfgnag gb chapgher, whfg gb nqq n
yvggyr cebgrpgvba. Nppbzcnalvat fyrrirf ({gyunlzrl}), bevt-
vanyyl abg cnegf bs gur ghavp vgfrys, jrer trarenyyl znqr bs
navzny crygf ({irQQVezrl}), fxva ({QVe}) jvgu she ({irQ}) fgvyy
nggnpurq. (Va zbqrea hfntr, gur jbeq {lViorU} va zbfg
cynprf zrnaf nal fuveg, jvgu be jvgubhg fyrrirf.) N jne-
evbe'f tybir ({cbtu}), nyfb znqr bs fxva, unq jvqr onaq
nebhaq gur jevfg naq funec cebgehfvbaf ng gur xahpxyrf.
Vs gurer jnf n fcrpvny anzr sbe gurfr cebgehfvbaf, vg vf
ybfg; gurl ner abj pnyyrq fvzcyl {QhDjV'zrl} ("fcvxrf").
Gur tybirf qvq abg unir svatref. Gurl jrer qrfvtarq gb
cebgrpg gur cnyz, onpx bs gur unaq, naq jevfg, ohg gb abg
vagresrer jvgu gur zbovyvgl bs n jneevbe'f svatref. Zbqrea
tybirf ({cbtuzrl}) trarenyyl nqurer gb guvf qrfvta. N fxva
oryg ({dbtu}) obgu uryq cnagf ({lbcjnU}) va cynpr naq ceb-
ivqrq n cynpr sebz juvpu gb unat jrncbaf be jrncba
ubyqref. Ba gur gbr bs rnpu uvtu obbg ({QnF}), yvxrjvfr
znqr bs navzny uvqr ({QVe}), jnf n pynjyvxr fcvxr pnyyrq n
{ch'}. Gur jbeq {ch'} abj zrnaf "cunfre," naq gur arjre
zrnavat cebonoyl qrirybcrq sebz gur byqre "fcvxr" or-
pnhfr bs gur yvtugavat fcrrq jvgu juvpu bar qryvirerq n
oybj jvgu gur funec {ch'}. Va pbagrzcbenel Xyvatba, gur
fcvxr ba gur gbr bs n obbg vf nyjnlf pnyyrq n {QnFch'}
("obbg fcvxr"), arire {ch'} nybar. Svanyyl, byq nezbe va-
pyhqrq urnqtrne bs fbzr xvaq nccneragyl pnyyrq n {zVi},
juvpu, va zbqrea Xyvatba, zrnaf "uryzrg." Gur jbeq
nyfb fheivirf va gur jbeq {zVi'n'} ("pebja"; yvgrenyyl, "ovt
uryzrg" be "terng uryzrg"), n prerzbavny urnqcvrpr jbea
ol fbzr Xyvatba rzcrebef.

[[vzntr]]

Gur <ong'yrgu> bs Xnuyrff vf erpbirerq ol Xbe (Wbua Pbyvpbf) naq

ol Xnuyrff gur Hasbetrggnoyr, gur sbhaqre bs gur Xyvatba
Rzcver, sebz n ybpx bs uvf unve qvccrq va zbygra ynin.
Xnuyrff perngrq gur anzr {orgyrU}, zrnavat "fjbeq bs
ubabe." Gur jbeq {orgyrU} vf npghnyyl na nepunvp sbez. Va
pbagrzcbenel Xyvatba, "fjbeq bs ubabe" jbhyq or {ongyu
'rgyu}, gubhtu guvf cuenfr vf hfrq nyzbfg rkpyhfviryl nf n
genafyngvba be rkcynangvba bs gur byqre jbeq, {orgyrU}.
     Gurer vf na rkgrafvir ibpnohynel sbe gur zbirf nffb-
pvngrq jvgu <ong'yrgu> hfr. Gb guehfg be yhatr gbjneq bar'f [[c.60]]
bccbarag, sbe rknzcyr, vf {wbc}. Gb qrsyrpg n guehfg---gung
vf, gb cneel---vf {jnl'}. Gb guehfg rvgure raq bs gur <ong'yrgu>
(nf bccbfrq gb gur ybat cneg bs gur oynqr) hcjneq vf
{punD}. Gb punatr gur nccebkvzngr bevragngvba bs gur
jrncba sebz ubevmbagny gb iregvpny vf {atby}; gur erirefr vf
{yri}. Gb fyvqr gur oynqr bs bar'f <ong'yrgu> nybat gur oynqr bs
gur bccbarag'f jrncba vf {QVw}. Gb gjvey be ebgngr gur <ong'-
yrgu> vf {wVezbU} naq gb gbff vg sebz bar unaq gb gur bgure
(gur fnzr jbeq vf hfrq jurgure yrsg gb evtug be evtug gb
yrsg) vf {onD}. Jura grnpuvat fbzrbar gb hfr gur <ong'yrgu,>
gur ghgbe jvyy fubhg bhg zbirzragf---sbe rknzcyr, {lVwbc!
lVjnl'!} ("Yhatr! Qrsraq!"). Trarenyyl va fhpu n fvghn-
gvba, ubjrire, gur ghgbe jvyy hfr gur fubegrarq sbez bs
gur ynathntr xabja nf Pyvccrq Xyvatba naq fxvc gur vz-

Vg vf vzcbegnag gb abgr gung gur ghgbe vf tvivat gur fghqrag
qverpg pbzznaqf ("Yhatr! Qrsraq!"), abg fubhgvat bhg
gur anzrf bs zbirzragf.
     N fznyyre, bar-unaqrq irefvba bs gur <ong'yrgu> vf gur
{zrdyrU}, eraqrerq va Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq nf <zrx'yrgu>.
Sbe n zvabevgl bs Xyvatbaf jub cebabhapr obgu {o} naq {z}
vqragvpnyyl, nf {z}, gur jbeqf {orgyrU} naq {zrdyrU} fbhaq
nyzbfg gur fnzr, rfcrpvnyyl jura fubhgrq va gur urng bs
onggyr. Orpnhfr bs gur vzcbegnapr bs gur <ong'yrgu> va Xyva-
tba genqvgvba, ubjrire, gurl unir gnxra gb pnyyvat gur
<ong'yrgu> {orgyrU dhi} (cebabhaprq {zrgyrU dhi}), be "uba-

"yblny <zrx'yrgu."> Nygubhtu {orgyrU dhi} zvtug or pbafvq-

gur wbo bs znvagnvavat gur qvfgvapgvba. Gur ybatre {orgyrU

nzbat Xyvatbaf jub cebabhapr {o} naq {z} qvfgvapgyl,
gubhtu abg nf serdhragyl nf gur bar-jbeq sbezf.
     Gur jbeq {'rgyu} vf hfrq sbe "fjbeq" va trareny, ohg vg
ernyyl zrnaf "oynqr" bs nal xvaq. Gur {'rgyu}, gura, vf n

     N {'rgyu}, rira vs cevznevyl n jrncba, znl or hfrq va

     Va napvrag gvzrf, n jneevbe bsgra jber n {Un'dhw} ("ony-

cevqr va qrfvtavat n jrncba gung abg bayl cresbezf jryy
naq cresrpgyl svgf gur unaq bs gur hfre ohg gung nyfb vf

ba gur fvqr bs gur obql, pbaarpgrq gb gur oryg. Gur jbeq

     Gur genqvgvbany Xyvatba nefrany nyfb vapyhqrf gur nk,

vf {'boznD}. Vgf unaqyr vf vgf {QrF} naq vgf oynqr vf vgf {tuVg}.

qbhoyr-urnqrq nk vf n {wrl'anF}, juvyr na nk jvgu na nqqrq [[c.64]]

hyngr gur {'ndyrU} vf {Dnpu}.
     N trareny grez sbe "fcrne" vf {anDwrw}, ohg, bs pbhefr,
gurer ner fcrpvsvp glcrf bs fcrnef. Gur {tuVagnd}, sbe rknz-
cyr, vf n onggyr fcrne, gubhtu vg vf nyfb hfrq prerzbavnyyl.
Gur funsg bs n fcrne vf gur {gVU}; gur funec gvc be fcrneurnq
vf gur {DVa}. Nf zvtug or rkcrpgrq, gurer ner n terng znal
qvssrerag glcrf bs {DVazrl} (gur cyheny sbez bs {DVa}). N

ab bgure fcrneurnqf ner anzrq jvgu ahzoref. N fcrne-

npghnyyl uvg vf gb nqq gur fhssvk {-puh'} ("cresrpgyl") gb gur
ireo: {wntu puhUpuh' FhijV'} ("Gur jneevbe fcrnef gur

{gyuriwnD}, juvpu rzcyblf n {purgiV'}, n fgvpx jvgu n ubbx [[c.65]]
ng gur raq, nf na nvq sbe guebjvat. Gurer vf n fvatyr ireo,
{jbo}, gung vf hfrq gb qrfpevor gur shyy enatr bs npgvivgvrf
vaibyirq va chggvat gur fcrne cebcreyl vagb gur fcrne- [[xrrc ulcura]]
guebjvat nvq naq hfvat gur nve gb uhey gur fcrne: {gyuriwnD [[nve:=nvq]]
jbo} ("Ur/fur chgf gur {gyuriwnD} vagb gur {purgiV'} naq
uheyf gur fcrne"). Va fcrnxvat bs guvf glcr bs fcrne naq

{puhU} jura gnyxvat nobhg guebjvat gur fcrne ng n gnetrg.
     Vg znl unir orra abgvprq gung fbzr bs gur grezvaby-
btl nffbpvngrq jvgu fcrnef vf vqragvpny gb gung nffbpvngrq
jvgu zbqrea jrncbael, naq pregnvayl gur ibpnohynel bs

     Bs fvzvyne funcr gb n fcrne, ohg hggreyl qvfgvapg, vf gur

vzcbegnag ebyr va gur {aragnl pun'QVpu}, be Frpbaq Evgr bs

[[vzntr]]

Punapryybe Tbexba (Qnivq Jneare) pneevrf n prerzbavny fgnss gung [[k!]]
gnxrf vgf sbez sebz gur napvrag {wrddVw}. <Oehpr Ovezryva> [[k!]]

}} [[c.67]]
baf vf gur {wrddVw}, gur pyho be oyhqtrba. Guvf jrncba vf
znqr bs jbbq, fbzrgvzrf jvgu vaynvq ebpxf, naq vf urni-
vre ng bar raq guna gur bgure. Vapyhqrq va guvf pngrtbel vf
gur {tunawnd}, bsgra genafyngrq nf "znpr," n pyho jvgu n
zrgny urnq, fbzrgvzrf fcbegvat fcvxrf ({QhDjV'zrl}). Nf
jvgu nkrf, gb jvryq be fjvat n pyho vf {Dnpu}.
     Nf cebgrpgvba ntnvafg gurfr inevbhf jrncbaf, n jne-
evbe bsgra pneevrq n fuvryq, be {lbQ}, onfvpnyyl n ynetr cyngr
bs zrgny. Gur ireo sbez bs "fuvryq" vf nyfb {lbQ}, naq gb
"fuvryq barfrys" vf {lbQ'rtu}. (Nygubhtu gur Srqrengvba
Fgnaqneq jbeq "fuvryqf" ersref gb obgu gur byq unaq-uryq
cebgrpgvir nezbe naq gur sbepr svryq cebgrpgvat n irffry---
gur arjre zrnavat pyrneyl onfrq ba gur byqre---va Xyva-
tba, gurer vf ab pbaarpgvba orgjrra gur gjb. Gur sbepr
svryq ba n fuvc vf pnyyrq {obgwna}. Gb fuvryq n fuvc, bar zhfg
"npgvingr gur fuvryqf," be {obgwna puh'}.)
     N jrncba gung vf cnegvphyneyl tbbq, gung vf jryy qr-
fvtarq naq jryy pbafgehpgrq, vf abeznyyl qrfpevorq nf
{inD}. Guhf, n {gnw inD} vf n zrgvphybhfyl znqr xavsr naq n
{tunawnd inD} vf na rfcrpvnyyl avpr znpr. Va fcrnxvat
nobhg n svar jrncba, bar pbhyq pbzcyvzrag vg rira she-
gure ol nqqvat gur rzcungvp {-dh'} gb {inD}. N ernyyl fcrpgnp-
hyne <ong'yrgu> jbhyq or n {orgyrU inDdh'}. Gur jbeq {inD} vf
abg bsgra hfrq va qrfpevovat gur arjre jrncbaf (qvfehcg-
bef naq gur yvxr), gubhtu fhpu ybphgvbaf ner urneq sebz
gvzr gb gvzr. Gur bevtvany zrnavat bs {inD} unf orra rk-
graqrq gb zrna "rssrpgvir, ivtbebhf, ntterffvir" naq vf
abj urneq nccyvrq abg bayl gb jrncbaf ohg nyfb gb crb-

ZHFVP

     Nygubhtu Xyvatba zhfvp vf cresbezrq engure vaser-
dhragyl bhgfvqr bs gur Rzcver, zhfvp cynlf n ivgny ebyr va

ybat pryroengrq terng npuvrirzragf naq xrl riragf va
fbat, ervasbepvat gur vzcbegnapr bs gur nppbzcyvfu-
zragf naq npghnyyl eryvivat gurz juvyr fvatvat. Terng
qrrqf ner "qrrqf jbegul bs fbat," nf gur Xyvatba yrnqre [[c.71]]
Tbjeba bapr chg vg, naq cneg bs gur nccrny bs ratntvat
va onggyr vf gur cebfcrpg gung, vs gur onggyr vf n ernyyl tbbq
bar, vg jvyy or sbhtug bire naq bire ntnva va fbat.
     Gur Xyvatba jbeq sbe zhfvp vf {DbD}. Guvf ersref gb
nal zhfvp, ibpny be vafgehzragny be obgu gbtrgure. N fbat

be "fbat jbeqf"). Gur jbeq sbe "cresbez zhfvp,"
jurgure vafgehzragny be ibpny naq vafgehzragny gb-
trgure, vf {zhpu}, juvpu va bgure pbagrkgf zrnaf "cerf-
rag," nf va "cerfrag n tvsg" gb fbzrbar. N zhfvpvna vf n
{zhpujV'} (yvgrenyyl, "bar jub cresbezf zhfvp"); n fvatre
vf n {obzjV'} ("bar jub fvatf").
     Gur jbeq hfrq sbe "pbzcbfr" vf {dba}. Guvf ireo nyfb
zrnaf "erpbeq" naq vf hfrq jurgure gur erpbeqvat vf ol
unaq (gung vf, jevggra be rira rgpurq va fgbar), va n zr-
qvhz fhvgnoyr sbe n pbzchgre, be nal bgure sbez. Sebz
gur Xyvatba cbvag bs ivrj, n fbat vf abg gur cebqhpg bs na
vaqvivqhny'f zvaq. Vg unf fbzrubj nyjnlf rkvfgrq naq vf

fbat erpbeqre, {dbajV'}) gb genafpevor vg ({dba}) naq gura

jryy xabja fbatjevgref, naq vg vf dhvgr na ubabe vs bar bs
gurz pbzcbfrf n fbat nobhg bar'f rkcybvgf. Pheeragyl,
creuncf gur zbfg erfcrpgrq {dbajV'} vf Xrrqren.
     Gubhtu bar bppnfvbanyyl urnef fbzrbar fnl {DbD gVi}
("Ur/fur rawblf [gur] zhfvp") be {obz gVi} ("Ur/fur rawblf
gur fbat"), zhfvp vf abg ernyyl pbafvqrerq fbzrguvat gung
pnhfrf cyrnfher. Nzbat Xyvatbaf, cyrnfher vf qrrzrq
dhvgr harffragvny sbe bar'f jryy-orvat. Zber serdhragyl,

ireo {QhD} (yvgrenyyl, "fgno"): {zhQhD obz} ("Gur fbat
fgnof zr," be, va n zber pbyybdhvny Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq
sbez, "Gur fbat zbirf zr"). Vs gur zhfvp vf whqtrq cbfv-

or {'rl}, hfvat gur jbeq abeznyyl genafyngrq nf "qryvpvbhf"

     Genqvgvbany Xyvatba zhfvp vf trarenyyl cresbezrq

fghql bs guvf glcr bs zhfvp, jurgure pbzcbfvgvba be cre-

Genqvgvbany Xyvatba zhfvpny sbezf qngr onpx gb gur gvzr

     Byqre Xyvatba zhfvp jnf onfrq ba n abangbavp

n fcrpvsvp anzr, pbzcnenoyr gb gur "qb, er, zv" flfgrz

{Fbpu,} "frira"; {pubetu,} "rvtug." Vg vf cbffvoyr gung, ng
fbzr gvzr va gur cnfg, gur ahzrenyf jrer "obeebjrq"

hfrq. Vg vf sne zber yvxryl, ubjrire, gung gur obeebjvat
jrag va gur bgure qverpgvba. Nf vf jryy qbphzragrq, gur

zny flfgrz (onfrq ba gra). Gur vaqrcraqrag jbeqf sbe

     Nzbat gur genqvgvbany zhfvpny sbezf vf jung unf

Gurer ner gubfr jub inel fbzrjung sebz gur gvtug fgehp-

aVg} (creuncf "tenaq bcren," gubhtu yvgrenyyl fbzrguvat

     Gur fgbevrf npgrq bhg va Xyvatba bcrenf znl or

Bppnfvbanyyl, na bcren cerfragf na bevtvany cybg. Gb sby-
ybj gur fgbel, bar unf gb cercner nurnq bs gvzr. Svefg bs

jbeqf) vf va na napvrag gbathr urneq abj bayl va gur bc-

     Xyvatba "cbchyne" zhfvp, sbe ynpx bs n orggre grez

     Jvaq vafgehzragf (gurer vf ab birenyy grez sbe gurz)

YNATHNTR PUNATR NAQ
FGNLVAT PHEERAG

Xyvatba fbpvrgl vf bar va juvpu genqvgvba cynlf n
uvtuyl fvtavsvpnag ebyr. Napvrag phfgbzf, evghnyf,
naq oryvrsf ner cnvafgnxvatyl, pbafpvragvbhfyl, naq fhp-
prffshyyl cnffrq ba sebz bar trarengvba gb gur arkg. Xyva-
tbaf erirer gurve naprfgbef, erfcrpg gurve ryqref, naq unir
hacnenyyryrq irarengvba sbe urevgntr. Arireguryrff, bire
gvzr, punatr qbrf bpphe va nyy nfcrpgf bs Xyvatba yvsr,
naq gurer ner bofreinoyr qvssreraprf---fbzr fhogyr, fbzr
engure boivbhf---orgjrra gur byqre naq lbhatre traren-
gvbaf. Gur zber rfgnoyvfurq zrzoref bs Xyvatba fbpvrgl
(trarenyyl fcrnxvat, byqre Xyvatbaf) graq gb frr punatr
nf vaqvpngvat gur tenqhny qbjasnyy bs gur fbpvrgl, gur ybff
bs inyhrf naq genqvgvbaf. "Gur jneevbe rguvp vf qrgrevbeng-
vat" vf n pbzzba ynzrag. Lbhatre Xyvatbaf, juvyr np-
prcgvat gurve urevgntr naq bofreivat gur napvrag evgrf, frr
fbzr nfcrpgf bs gurve ryqref' orunivbe naq oryvrsf nf, vs
abg bofbyrgr, gura whfg byq-snfuvbarq. Guvf fgngr bs nssnvef
jnf abg oebhtug ba ol erprag grpuabybtvpny vaabingvba
fhpu nf tnynpgvp geniry; vg unf orra guvf jnl sbe praghevrf.
     Gur qvssreraprf orgjrra lbhatre naq byqre Xyvatbaf
ner zveeberq va gur jnl zrzoref bs gur qvssrerag traren-
gvbaf fcrnx. Juvyr rirelbar qbrf fcrnx gur fnzr yna-
thntr (naq guvf qvfphffvba vf erfgevpgrq gb {gn' Uby}, gur
fgnaqneq qvnyrpg), gurer ner fgvyy pregnva fcrrpu cnggreaf
pyrneyl nffbpvngrq jvgu lbhatre fcrnxref, naq bgure cng- [[c.136]]
greaf jvgu byqre. Cnenyyryvat gur qvssrevat nggvghqrf nobhg
bgure nfcrpgf bs fbpvrgl, gur Xyvatba fcbxra ol byqre
zrzoref bs fbpvrgl vf pbafvqrerq ol fbzr gb or "cebcre
naq rybdhrag" naq ol bguref gb or "fgvygrq naq pbasvavat";
gur Xyvatba fcbxra ol gur lbhatre trarengvba vf rvgure
"fybccl naq hatenzzngvpny" be "vaabingvir naq rkcerf-
fvir." Gubhtu vg vf fnsr gb fnl gung zhpu bs guvf vaabin-
gvba vf urneq nzbat lbhatre fcrnxref, gurer vf ab pyrne
yvar bs qrznexngvba frcnengvat gur trarengvbaf, ab ntr ng
juvpu bar pebffrf bire sebz "lbhatre" gb "byqre." Nggv-
ghqr naq fgnxr va gur fgnghf dhb cynl terngre ebyrf guna
qbrf puebabybtvpny ntr. Vaqrrq, gurer vf n terng qrny bs
qvfnterrzrag nf gb juvpu arjre srngherf bs gur ynathntr
(trarenyyl, gubfr nffbpvngrq jvgu lbhatre Xyvatbaf) ner
npprcgnoyr vaabingvbaf naq juvpu ner fvzcyl reebef. Vg vf
gurersber cebonoyl orfg sbe gur ivfvgbe gb nibvq gnxvat n
fgnaq ba jung vf "pbeerpg" Xyvatba naq, jura nfxrq gb
frggyr n qvfchgr, gb qrsre gb gur jvfqbz bs gur angvir
fcrnxref, nyy bs jubz rawbl n tbbq svtug naljnl.
     Qrcraqvat hcba bar'f ntr (be, zber vzcbegnagyl,
hcba gur ntr tebhc jvgu juvpu bar zbfg vqragvsvrf), bar
znl be znl abg jnag gb nqbcg gur cebahapvngvba cng-
greaf be tenzzngvpny crphyvnevgvrf nffbpvngrq jvgu gur
lbhatre trarengvba. Vg vf jbegujuvyr sbe n ivfvgbe gb or
snzvyvne jvgu gurfr cnggreaf, ubjrire, vs sbe ab bgure ern-
fba guna gb or noyr gb haqrefgnaq jung n lbhatre Xyva-
tba vf fnlvat.
     Jura vg pbzrf gb ibpnohynel, ba gur bgure unaq,
xabjyrqtr bs cerinvyvat grezvabybtl vf rffragvny vs bar
vf gb haqrefgnaq naq cnegvpvcngr va rirelqnl pbairefn-
gvba. Gurer ner jbeqf naq rkcerffvbaf, hfhnyyl qhoorq
<fynat>, gung ner vaserdhragyl hfrq va fpubyneyl be fpvra-
gvsvp jevgvat be va sbezny cerfragngvbaf, fhpu nf whqvpvny
cebprrqvatf be tbireazragny prerzbavrf, ohg gurl ner
dhvgr pbzzba bgurejvfr, obgu va pbairefngvba naq va
cbchyne jevgvat, fhpu nf ebznapr abiryf. Fhpu jbeqf
ner bsgra abg vapyhqrq va grkgobbxf be va pynffebbz [[c.137]]

vafgehpgvba orpnhfr gurl ner abg pbafvqrerq "cebcre."

TRARENGVBANY QVSSRERAPRF:
CEBAHAPVNGVBA NAQ TENZZNE

     Gur qvssreraprf va cebahapvngvba orgjrra lbhatre
naq byqre Xyvatbaf ner engure fhogyr. Nf n erfhyg, gur
punenpgrevfgvp cnggreaf bs lbhatre crbcyr'f fcrrpu, vs ab-
gvprq naq pbzzragrq hcba, ner zber yvxryl gb or whqtrq
"fybccl" be "pneryrff" engure guna "jebat." Svefg bs nyy,
fbzr lbhatre fcrnxref graq gb cebabhapr qbhoyrq pba-
fbanagf nf vs gurl jrer fvatyr, juvyr byqre fcrnxref cerggl
zhpu znvagnva gur qvfgvapgvba orgjrra fvatyr naq qbh-
oyrq pbafbanagf. Sbe rknzcyr, va gur jbeq {drggnU} ("Ur/
fur xrrcf ba ehaavat"; {drg,} "eha, wbt," cyhf {-gnU,} "pbagva-
hbhf"), na byqre Xyvatba jbhyq rvgure cebabhapr rnpu {g}
qvfgvapgyl, eryrnfvat gur svefg bar jvgu n chss bs nve orsber
negvphyngvat gur frpbaq, be ryfr ur be fur jbhyq ubyq gur
{g} whfg n ovg orsber eryrnfvat vg, fb gung gur gvzr gnxra hc

hfrq bayl va fhpu fvghngvbaf. Sbe rknzcyr, n pncgnva'f
pbzznaq gb sver n gbecrqb vf zbfg pbzzbayl whfg {onU!}
("Sver [n gbecrqb]!") engure guna {lVonU!,} gur shyy sbez
jvgu gur vzcrengvir cersvk {lV-,} be rira gur yratguvre naq
zber rkcyvpvg {crat lVonU!} ("Sver gur gbecrqb!") Va gur
guebrf bs onggyr, ol gur gvzr gur beqre gb sver n gbecrqb vf
tvira, nyy pbaprearq ner rkcrpgvat gb urne gung beqre. Gur
gbecrqb unf nyernql orra ybnqrq vagb gur gbecrqb ghor,
gur jrncba unf orra nvzrq, naq gur svevat zrpunavfz
unf orra ernqvrq. Nyy gung vf yrsg vf sbe gur thaare gb npgh-
nyyl qvfpunetr gur jrncba. Guhf, gur bayl vasbezngvba
gung zhfg or pbairlrq ng guvf cbvag vf jura gb sver; gur
crefba qbvat gur svevat naq gur bowrpg gb or sverq ner ny-
ernql xabja ol nyy. Pyvccrq Xyvatba nppbzzbqngrf guvf
arrq dhvgr avpryl.
     Ba gur bgure unaq, vg jbhyq or vanccebcevngr gb hfr
Pyvccrq Xyvatba jura svefg beqrevat n qevax ng n one. Gb
nccebnpu gur onegraqre naq fnl fvzcyl {dnat!} ("Cbhe!")
qbrf abg pbairl rabhtu vasbezngvba. Jung fubhyq or
cbherq? Qbrf gur fcrnxre jnag gur onegraqre gb cbhe gur
qevax, be qbrf gur fcrnxre jnag gb qb vg uvz- be urefrys?
Bapr n pbagrkg unf orra rfgnoyvfurq, ubjrire, gur
pyvccrq pbzznaq sbez jbexf nqrdhngryl. Guhf, vs gur
onegraqre unf nyernql cbherq gjb be guerr tynffrf bs
oybbqjvar sbe n cngeba naq gurfr unir orra pbafhzrq,
gur phfgbzre'f fubhg bs {dnat!} jbhyq cebonoyl or pbe-
erpgyl vagrecergrq nf "Cbhe zr bar zber qevax bs oybbq-
jvar!"
     Gur ebyr bs pbagrkg va qrgrezvavat jurgure gb hfr
Pyvccrq Xyvatba vf obgu pehpvny naq fhogyr. Sbe rknzcyr,
va gur one fpranevb zragvbarq nobir, gb beqre na nqqv-

cnegvphyne pbaabgngvba. Ba gur bgure unaq, vs gur cngeba [[c.175]]
unq hfrq gur pyvccrq sbez ba bar be zber bppnfvbaf naq,
sbe fbzr ernfba, jnf qvfcyrnfrq jvgu gur onegraqre'f er-
fcbafr, hfr bs gur ybatre sbez gur arkg gvzr jbhyq pba-

gurer vf ab zvfhaqrefgnaqvat guvf gvzr: cbhe gur oybbq-
jvar." Fhpu n fjvgpu sebz Pyvccrq Xyvatba gb gur shyyre
sbez vf bsgra vagrecergrq nf n punyyratr gb bar'f ubabe,

jvgu gur pbafrdhraprf.
     Pyvccrq Xyvatba vf nyfb serdhragyl sbhaq va fbat yle-
vpf. Gurer ner gjb cbffvoyr ernfbaf sbe guvf. Svefg, fbatf
ner bsgra nffbpvngrq jvgu fvghngvbaf va juvpu fcbxra

gref!" Va gur fbat, gur svefg jbeq va rnpu yvar vf {Dbl}

     Npghnyyl, gurfr ylevpf ner na vyyhfgengvba bs nabgure

bar npprcgf fhpu pbafgehpgvbaf nf tenzzngvpny; gurve va-
nccebcevngrarff, gur jnl gurl tengr ba gur Xyvatba rne,
vf rknpgyl jung tvirf gurz rybphgvbanel pybhg. N ivfvgbe
znl urne bar bs gurfr bqq fhssvkrf bppnfvbanyyl, ohg, nf
jvgu bgure vagragvbanyyl hatenzzngvpny sbezf, vg vf orfg

jvgu gur ahnaprf bs Xyvatba fglyr.

NIBVQVAT TNSSRF

Qrfcvgr gur qvirefvgl rkuvovgrq ol fcrnxref bs Xyva-
tba jub orybat gb qvssrerag tebhcf be jub pbzr
sebz qvssrerag cnegf bs gur Rzcver, qrfcvgr gur npprcg-
novyvgl bs qvssrerag cebahapvngvbaf, grezvabybtl, naq
rira tenzzne, gurer ner fgvyy fbzr nfcrpgf bs ynathntr
hfr sbe juvpu gur fcrnxre zhfg or fher gb nqurer gb nyy
gur ehyrf engure zrgvphybhfyl. Sbe rknzcyr, pner zhfg or
gnxra jura cebabhapvat fbzr jbeqf naq cuenfrf gb ra-
fher gung gurl pnaabg or zvfgnxra sbe bgure jbeqf be
cuenfrf jvgu pbzcyrgryl qvssrerag zrnavatf. Jura
pubbfvat jbeqf, bar zhfg or njner gung gurer ner rkcerf-
fvbaf gung znl or hfrq jura fcrnxvat gb pregnva crbcyr
ohg zhfg or nibvqrq jura fcrnxvat gb bguref. Va nqqv-
gvba, jura genafyngvat gb be sebz Xyvatba, gurer ner fbzr
pbaprcgf gung graq gb pnhfr n pregnva nzbhag bs qvssvphygl
fvzcyl orpnhfr gurer ner ab jbeqf sbe gur pbaprcg va bar
be gur bgure bs gur ynathntrf. Guvf znl erfhyg va hatenz-
zngvpny pbafgehpgvbaf jubfr hfr pyrneyl znexf bar nf na
bhgfvqre naq gurersber cebonoyl nf bar abg gb or gehfgrq.
Vg vf vzcbegnag sbe nalbar ivfvgvat n Xyvatba frggyrzrag
gb or njner gung fnlvat gur jebat guvat be fnlvat vg va
gur jebat jnl znl abg bayl yrnq gb pbzzhavpngvba qvs-
svphygvrf ohg nyfb znl or qrgevzragny gb bar'f urnygu. [[c.188]]


CUBARGVP CREVYF

     Jura yrneavat gb fcrnx n arj ynathntr, bar unf n
graqrapl gb cebabhapr fbhaqf va n snzvyvne, pbzsbegnoyr
jnl, nf vs gurl jrer fbhaqf va n ynathntr nyernql fcbxra.
Sbe rknzcyr, fbzrbar jub fcrnxf Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq
znl zvfcebabhapr Xyvatba {d} nf <x> orpnhfr gur gjb
fbhaqf ner fvzvyne naq gur Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq fcrnxre
vf npphfgbzrq gb znxvat gur <x> fbhaq gbjneq gur onpx bs
gur zbhgu ohg vf abg npphfgbzrq gb znxvat n {d} fbhaq
rira snegure onpx. Va gur fnzr snfuvba, n Srqrengvba
Fgnaqneq fcrnxre znl zvfcebabhapr Xyvatba {Q}, znqr
jvgu gur gvc bs gur gbathr gbhpuvat gur ebbs bs gur zbhgu,
nf vs vg jrer gur fvzvyne ohg abg vqragvpny Srqrengvba Fgna-
qneq <q>, znqr jvgu gur gvc bs gur gbathr fbzrjung oruvaq
gur hccre grrgu. Hayrff gur Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq fcrnxre
yrneaf gb birepbzr byq unovgf, gura, ur be fur vf yvxryl gb
cebabhapr gur jbeq {dbQ} ("vagrevbe"), juvpu unf hasnzvy-
vne pbafbanagf, nf vs vg jrer Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq <pbqr>.
Gb cebabhapr Xyvatba jbeqf jvgu Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq
fbhaqf vf gb fcrnx Xyvatba jvgu n Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq
npprag. Sbe gur zbfg cneg, fcrnxvat Xyvatba jvgu na nyvra
npprag jvyy abg yrnq gb nal zvfhaqrefgnaqvat. Vs bar jrer
gb fnl <cn pbqr> sbe Xyvatba {cn' dbQ} ("ebbz'f vagrevbe, va-
fvqr bs n ebbz"), bar'f cebahapvngvba jbhyq orgenl uvf be
ure aba-Xyvatba fgnghf, naq bar jbhyq evfx orvat whqtrq
gbb ynml gb yrnea Xyvatba cebcreyl, ohg gur vqrn bs "vafvqr
bs n ebbz" jbhyq fgvyy or pbairlrq.
     Zvfcebahapvngvba znl ghea qnatrebhf, ba gur bgure
unaq, vs bar Xyvatba fbhaq vf fhofgvghgrq sbe nabgure.
Guvf vf zbfg yvxryl gb unccra vs obgu bs gur fbhaqf ner
vavgvnyyl hasnzvyvne gb gur ynathntr yrneare---gung vf, vs
gurl ner ynpxvat sebz gur yrneare'f angvir gbathr. Sbe rk-
nzcyr, gur Xyvatba fbhaqf {U} naq {D} ner abg sbhaq va Srq-
rengvba Fgnaqneq, naq fbzr fghqragf bs Xyvatba ng svefg
unir n uneq gvzr qvfgvathvfuvat gur gjb, rira gubhtu
gurl ner, gb n Xyvatba'f rne, dhvgr qvfgvapg. (Gur {D} unf n
fhqqra bafrg, vf cebqhprq snegure onpx va gur zbhgu, naq
vf ybhqre guna vf {U}.) Vs {D} vf zvfhfrq sbe {U} be ivpr irefn, [[c.189]]
bar zvtug nppvqragnyyl fnl {oVwrU} ("Lbh ner nofrag-
zvaqrq") jura bar vagraqf gb fnl {oVwrD} ("Lbh ner frys- [[xrrc ulcura]]
pbasvqrag"), be creuncf bar jvyy vffhr gur pbzznaq {lV-
Dbgyu!} ("Qvfnoyr vg!") jura bar vagraqf {lVUbgyu!} ("Fpna
vg!") Qrcraqvat ba gur pvephzfgnaprf, fhpu hggrenaprf
pbhyq or sngny reebef sbe gur fcrnxre.
     Fbzrgvzrf rira fbhaqf snzvyvne gb n ynathntr
yrneare pnhfr ceboyrzf. Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq fcrnxref
trarenyyl unir ab ceboyrz qvfgvathvfuvat gur Xyvatba
ibjry fbhaqf {r} naq {V} fvzcyl orpnhfr gurfr fbhaqf ner
qvfgvapg va Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq nf jryy (sbe rknzcyr, <crg>
irefhf <cvg>). Arireguryrff, jura bar vf yrneavat Xyvatba
jbeqf, vg vf abg hapbzzba gb pbashfr jbeqf jvgu {r} jvgu
jbeqf jvgu {V}, whfg nf va fbzr qvnyrpgf bs Srqrengvba Fgna-
qneq <cra> naq <cva> fbhaq cerggl zhpu nyvxr. Nyy gbb ser-
dhragyl, bar urnef ehzbef nobhg gur sngr bs n fghqrag bs
Xyvatba jub vagraqrq gb fnl {lb' dVw} ("Oynpx Syrrg") ohg
nppvqragnyyl fnvq {lb' drw} ("tebhpul syrrg") vafgrnq. (Va
Xyvatba zlgubybtl, gur Oynpx Syrrg vf n onaq pbafvfgvat
bs jneevbef jub unir qvrq oeniryl naq ubabenoyl naq, va
n fbeg bs nsgreyvsr, pneel ba tybevbhf onggyrf sberire.)
     Nf n cenpgvpny znggre, zbfg zvfcebahapvngvbaf jvyy
abg pnhfr ceboyrzf, fvzcyl orpnhfr pbagrkg jvyy znxr
bar jbeq engure guna gur bgure gur bayl cbffvoyr pubvpr.
Guhf, vs gur bpphcnag bs n ebbz urneq n qbbe puvzr,
gurer jbhyq cebonoyl or ab zvfhaqrefgnaqvat nf n erfhyg
bs uvf be ure fnlvat {lV'Vy!} ("Or fvaprer!") engure guna gur
pbeerpg {lV'ry!} ("Ragre!"). Va gur fvghngvba ng unaq, bayl
"Ragre!" znxrf nal frafr. Fbzrgvzrf tenzzne znxrf
gur pbagrkg pyrne. Sbe rknzcyr, fnlvat {wbDch'} engure guna
{wbUch'} sbe "Ybeqf, Ynqvrf" ({wbU,} "Ybeq, Ynql"; {-ch',} cyh-
eny fhssvk) cebonoyl jbhyq abg or zvfvagrecergrq nf fnl-
vat "evof" ({wbD,} "evo") orpnhfr gur cyheny fhssvk {-ch'} vf
hfrq bayl jvgu abhaf vaqvpngvat orvatf pncnoyr bs hfvat
ynathntr. Gur erirefr vf yvxrjvfr gehr. Gung vf, vs bar fnvq
{wbUQh'} engure guna {wbDQh'} sbe "evof," gur zrnavat bs
"evof" jbhyq cebonoyl or haqrefgbbq orpnhfr gur cyheny [[c.190]]
fhssvk {-Qh'} vf hfrq bayl sbe obql cnegf. Va vqragvpny snfu-
vba, zvfcebabhapvat {wbUjV'} ("zl Ybeq" be "zl Ynql")
nf {wbDjV'} jbhyq cebonoyl abg pnhfr gur yvfgrare gb guvax
gung "zl evo" jnf gur vagraqrq zrnavat, orpnhfr gur fhs-
svk {-jV'} ("zl") vf hfrq bayl jvgu abhaf pncnoyr bs hfvat
ynathntr. Gur fhssvk zrnavat "zl" hfrq jvgu bgure
abhaf vf {-jVw}, nf va {wbDjVw} ("zl evo"). Gb fgnl bhg bs gebh-
oyr, ubjrire, vg vf vzcbegnag gb trg gur tenzzne evtug.
Vs, sbe vafgnapr, bar qvq abg haqrefgnaq gur nccebcevngr
hfntrf bs gur cyheny fhssvkrf {-ch'} irefhf {-Qh'} be bs gur
cbffrffvir fhssvkrf {-jV'} irefhf {-jVw}, gurer pbhyq or hasbe-
ghangr ercrephffvbaf rira vs bar'f cebahapvngvba jrer
cresrpg. Nqqerffvat "zl Ybeq" be "zl Ynql" nf {wbUjVw}
engure guna {wbUjV'} vf vafhygvat vaqrrq, fvapr vg vzcyvrf
gung "zl Ybeq" be "zl Ynql" vf n ybjre beqre bs orvat.
Fvzvyneyl, n tebhc bs urnqf bs ubhfrubyqf jbhyq cebon-
oyl abg nccerpvngr orvat ersreerq gb nf {wbUQh'}, fvapr gung
jbhyq or gur nccebcevngr jnl gb fnl "Ybeqf" be "Ynqvrf"
bayl vs gurl jrer obql cnegf. Gur bayl guvat jbefr jbhyq
or pbzovavat zvfcebahapvngvba jvgu tenzzngvpny oyha-
qrevat, fhpu nf ol fnlvat {wbDQh'jVw} ("zl evof")---jvgu {D}
engure guna {U,} {-Qh'} engure guna {-ch'}, naq {-jVw} engure
guna {-jV'}---jura {wbUch'jV'} ("zl Ybeqf, zl Ynqvrf") vf
vagraqrq. Zvfgnxrf bs guvf xvaq ner fvzcyl abg gbyrengrq
naq gurer ner ab erpbeqrq vafgnaprf bs nalbar yvivat ybat
rabhtu gb ercrng gur bssrafr.
     Bs pbhefr, abg nyy cebahapvngvba reebef ner rtertvbhf.
Fbzr cebqhpr frznagvpnyyl crphyvne hggrenaprf naq,
gurersber, ner hfhnyyl erpbtavmnoyr nf reebef. Guhf, vs n
jbhyq-or pncgnva jrer gb fubhg {lVonD!} engure guna
{lVonU!} ("Sver [gur gbecrqb]!"; {onU,} "sver [n gbecrqb]"), ur
be fur jbhyq or fnlvat "Or whfg cvpxrq!" Gur pbafr-
dhraprf bs fhpu na reebe jbhyq or gevivny, ubjrire, fvapr
gur ireo {onD} ("or serfu, whfg cvpxrq") nccyvrf bayl gb sehvg
be irtrgnoyrf naq vf hggreyl vapbatehbhf va gur pbagrkg bs
gbecrqb ynhapuvat. Vaqrrq, fvapr {lVonU} vf jung bar
jbhyq rkcrpg gb urne va fhpu n fvghngvba, gur zvfcebaha-
pvngvba jbhyq cebonoyl tb haabgvprq be ryfr or pbafvq-
rerq n zrer fyvc bs gur gbathr. [[c.191]]
     Ba gur bgure unaq, bar fubhyq abg eryl ba pbagrkg be
frznagvp jrveqarff nf nyjnlf orvat ninvynoyr gb onvy bar
bhg bs n fgvpxl fvghngvba gung erfhygf sebz negvphyngvat n
jbeq vapbeerpgyl. Jura qrnyvat jvgu Xyvatbaf, vg vf fnsrfg
gb nibvq chggvat barfrys va fhpu n fvghngvba va gur svefg
cynpr ol orvat njner bs juvpu zvfcebahapvngvbaf bar vf
zbfg yvxryl gb znxr. Gb gung raq, gur sbyybjvat frpgvbaf
pbagnva cnvef bs jbeqf naq cuenfrf bs juvpu gb or cnegvp-
hyneyl jnel. Gur yvfgf ner ol ab zrnaf pbzcyrgr naq ner
jrvtugrq va snibe bs gur zvfgnxrf zbfg pbzzba nzbat
gubfr jubfr svefg ynathntr vf Srqrengvba Fgnaqneq. Gur
orfg pbhefr bs npgvba sbe n ivfvgbe gb n Xyvatba cynarg vf
gb nffhzr gung nyy zvfcebahapvngvbaf yrnq gb gebhoyr naq
gb or pnershy jvgu rahapvngvba haqre nyy pvephzfgnaprf.

     Svanyyl, gurer ner fbzr jbeqf gung fvzcyl qb abg

NOBHG GUR NHGUBE

ZNEP BXENAQ qrivfrq gur qvnybthr naq pbnpurq gur npgbef fcrnxvat
gur Xyvatba[GZ] ynathntr urneq va <Fgne Gerx VVV: Gur Frnepu sbe Fcbpx>[GZ],
<Fgne Gerx I: Gur Svany Sebagvre>[GZ], naq <Fgne Gerx IV: Gur Haqvfpbirerq
Pbhagel>[GZ]. Gur Xyvatba ynathntr ur qrirybcrq unf nyfb orra hfrq va n
ahzore bs rcvfbqrf bs <Fgne Gerx: Gur Arkg Trarengvba>, <Fgne Gerx: Qrrc
Fcnpr Avar>, naq <Fgne Gerx: Iblntre>[GZ]. Va nqqvgvba, ur perngrq gur Ihypna
qvnybthr sbe <Fgne Gerx VV: Gur Jengu bs Xuna>, nf jryy nf <Fgne Gerx VVV>. [[VVV:=VVV: Gur Frnepu sbe Fcbpx]]

Ur vf gur nhgube bs <Gur Xyvatba Qvpgvbanel> (Cbpxrg Obbxf, 1985; erivfrq
rqvgvba, 1992), na vagebqhpgvba gb gur tenzzne naq ibpnohynel bs gur
ynathntr, naq <Gur Xyvatba Jnl: N Jneevbe'f Thvqr> (Cbpxrg Obbxf, 1996), na
naabgngrq pbzcvyngvba bs Xyvatba cebireof. Ur pna or urneq qrfpevovat
inevbhf nfcrpgf bs gur ynathntr naq vgf rssrpgvir hfr ba gur
nhqvbpnffrggrf <Pbairefngvbany Xyvatba> (Fvzba & Fpuhfgre Nhqvbjbexf, [[nhqvbpnffrggrf:=nhqvb pnffrggrf]]
1992) naq <Cbjre Xyvatba> (pbjevggra jvgu Oneel Yrivar, Fvzba &
Fpuhfgre Nhqvbjbexf, 1993), obgu aneengrq ol Zvpunry Qbea. Ur nyfb
qrivfrq Xyvatba qvnybthr naq pbagevohgrq gb gur ynathntr yno cbegvba
bs gur PQ-EBZ <Fgne Gerx: Xyvatba> (Fvzba & Fpuhfgre Vagrenpgvir, 1996).

Ur unf qrterrf va yvathvfgvpf sebz gur Fnagn Pehm naq Orexryrl
pnzchfrf bs gur Havirefvgl bs Pnyvsbeavn naq unf pbaqhpgrq yvathvfgvp
erfrnepu nf n cbfgqbpgbeny sryybj ng gur Fzvgufbavna Vafgvghgvba va
Jnfuvatgba, Q.P. Va nqqvgvba gb uvf jbex ba Xyvatba, ur unf jevggra
negvpyrf ba yvathvfgvpf sbe frireny wbheanyf naq nagubybtvrf. [[c.onpx pbire]]

XYVATBA SBE GUR TNYNPGVP GENIRYRE
lbh jvyy xabj.

Betnavmrq vagb sbhe rnfl-gb-hfr frpgvbaf, guvf obbx jvyy thvqr lbhe fgrcf
guebhtu gur Xyvatba ynathntr naq phfgbzf:
 Gur ertvbany qvnyrpgf bs gur Rzcver
 Pbzzba, rirelqnl hfntr bs gur ynathntr
 Gur fynat cuenfrf naq phefrf gung pbybe gur Xyvatba ibpnohynel
 Zbfg vzcbegnagyl, gur cebcre ireony, culfvpny, naq phygheny erfcbafrf.

N zvffcbxra jbeq gb n Xyvatba, jub vf dhvpx gb gnxr bssrafr naq rira
dhvpxre gb gnxr npgvba, pbhyq unir qver pbafrdhraprf. Guvf obbx vf gur
vaqvfcrafnoyr thvqr sbe gur tnynpgvp geniryre.
